Song Ziwen Speaks on Developing Hainan Island

(Guangzhou) Song Ziwen delivered a speech at the welcoming rally in Wenchang on the 3rd. The original text is as follows: Chairman, elders, brothers, and sisters, although I am from Hainan Island, I have never returned to my hometown. Today, arriving in Wenchang and meeting with all of you fellow villagers is truly the most joyful thing in my life. At the same time, I hold infinite hope for my hometown. This visit to Hainan Island is not just a tour of my homeland; it is with Commander-in-Chief Yu, Vice Minister Zeng, Commander Chen, Director Song, and other officials to Hainan Island, all embracing the implementation of the late Premier's instructions on national defense and economic construction. Since the Premier advocated the development of Hainan Island, countless people have continued to propose it, believing that Hainan Island has endowed resources and that the people of Hainan Island have the most courage. They can develop their own hometown, but until now, it has not been realized. Speaking of this, I have a feeling: hundreds of thousands of Hainanese people travel far overseas, and the money they earn from their hard work is continuously remitted back to the motherland, which shows that they do have the ability. In particular, they have recovered a lot of leakage for the country in terms of trade deficits, which is extremely admirable and praiseworthy. However, the reason why they develop outward despite the long distance is that they are oppressed by the environment and the economy at home and have to endure hardships and travel across the ocean to seek a way out in foreign lands among foreign races. We Hainanese people are very similar to the Irish in Europe. There is no place for them to live in their hometowns, and they can only exchange blood and sweat for food and clothing abroad. This kind of perseverance to fight and take risks instead of sitting still and waiting for death is the true courage of the Hainanese people. Since Hainan Island is endowed with natural resources and possesses a nation with perseverance, why has it not been developed until now? In my observation, there are three major obstacles. The first obstacle is the issue of public security. Since the Republic of China, Hainan Island has been ravaged by Long Jiguang, Deng Benyin, and the Communist Party, and the subsequent Guangdong authorities have paid no attention to Hainan Island as if it were a remote foreign land. Whenever there was trouble on the mainland, they would transfer all the garrison troops away, and they did not carefully select honest and capable officials in politics, which resulted in bandits everywhere and people living in misery for several years. Well-to-do overseas Chinese naturally did not dare to return home, and poor villagers had no choice but to migrate abroad. Now, everyone has admitted that Hainan Island is an important area in terms of national defense. The purpose of Commander-in-Chief Yu stationing a large army is not only for local public security but also for the needs of national defense. I firmly believe that no matter what happens in the future, there will be sufficient military force to protect the local area so that everyone can live and work in peace. This is something I can tell the elders. The second obstacle is the political issue. In recent years, domestic politics has been bad, as everyone knows, and there is nothing to hide. Our Hainan Island is isolated in the sea, and the officials governing the county are like the saying goes, "The sky is high and the emperor is far away," and they carry out tyrannical politics and arbitrary exploitation. The people of the countryside suffer from the devastation of bad politics even more than their compatriots on the mainland. Today, Commander-in-Chief Yu and all the military and civilian officials have come to our hometown, and Director Song also has the mission of Minister Kong, all for the purpose of seeing the suffering of the people and seeking welfare for our villages. It has been decided to abolish the salt monopoly and continue to eliminate all kinds of exorbitant taxes. Commissioner Huang is a local administrative official with rich experience and new knowledge. He has had the greatest enthusiasm for the development of Hainan Island for more than ten years. I firmly believe that he will be able to implement the various plans of the central and local military and political officials to purify officialdom and eliminate corrupt practices. The third obstacle is the transportation issue. We know that the biggest key to developing any region is to solve the transportation problem first. There is no seaport construction along the coast of Hainan Island, and there is no railway transportation in the hinterland. This time, Commander-in-Chief Yu, Railway Minister Zeng, Director Song, Commissioner Huang, and I have discussed several times and have established basic transportation plans. Moreover, the development of Hainan Island has a major connection with national defense and economy. Using the financial resources of various provinces to help complete the transportation plan will definitely be possible. Based on the above, the three major obstacles to the development of Hainan Island can be removed by some means. The so-called favorable weather, geographical advantages, and harmony among the people have all come together. My fellow villagers can rely on their own efforts to work hard for their hometown and for the party and the country, without having to work for others and develop in foreign lands. And my overseas Chinese can use their capital and experience to come back and serve their hometown. Today, I am honored to be invited by the conference. I was originally scheduled to arrive at two o'clock, but I was delayed along the way, and it was too late to arrive in Wenchang. I am very sorry for making you fellow villagers wait so hard. The reason for the delay was that I took a plane around the island and flew over the Wuzhi Mountain to observe the situation, which took more time. But this made me think of the past when I wanted to circle the island and climb the Wuzhi Mountain, which could not be completed in one or two months. Today, it can be achieved in three hours. This proves that what could not be done in the past can now be done, and what was very difficult in the past is now easy. This is the most accurate and best metaphor for the development of Hainan Island. I believe that under the leadership of the central government, Commander-in-Chief Yu, Chairman Huang, and other officials, with the help of the national economic strength, and with the courage of my millions of fellow villagers who have developed Southeast Asia, transferred to their hometown, and working together, the results in the next three to five years will definitely exceed the progress of the previous thirty to fifty years. I also believe that we can realize the late Premier's instructions on developing Hainan Island in the shortest possible time. I am a part of Hainan Island. Although I had the desire to develop it in the past, it was only based on an ideal. Today, when I actually arrived in my hometown, I felt infinite emotion in my mind. Under the guidance of implementing the late Premier's instructions and in the desire of the fellow villagers returning to Hainan Island and the compatriots of the whole country, I will devote all my efforts at any time and place to follow everyone to achieve success. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Legislative Yuan Meeting Passes the Organizational Law of the Department of Health, The Proposal to Add a Deputy Director-General Fails to Pass

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its eighty-second meeting on the morning of the 4th, with 69 members including Wang Kunlun present. Sun Ke presided as Chairman, with Liang Han Cao as Secretary-General. The agenda included: (1) The proposal that labor creditors should have the highest priority of repayment. Resolution: Passed according to the review report of the Civil Law Committee, and the case was handed over to the Labor Law Committee to add provisions when drafting the Labor Contract Law. (2) Amendment to the Organizational Law of the Department of Health. Resolution: Passed with amendments according to the review report of the Legal Affairs Committee. (3) Amendment to the Chinese Medicine Ordinance. Resolution: Passed with amendments according to the review report of the Legal Affairs Committee. (4) The Labor Law Committee reported on the drafting of the Labor Contract Law. Due to time constraints, only the second reading was passed. Chapter 1 of the law, General Provisions, consisted of seven articles. The original provision in the General Provisions chapter, "If a wife's labor for others is detrimental to the interests of her family, the husband may revoke it," was deleted according to the motion of Lin Gengbai, Wei Tingsheng, Chen Changheng, etc., to prevent the husband's rights from being higher than the wife's and to maintain gender equality. The other four chapters on the obligations of laborers, the obligations of employers, the termination of labor contracts, penalties, and supplementary provisions were left for discussion at the next Yuan meeting. In addition, the amended Organizational Law of the Department of Health has 13 articles. The main points of the amendment are to add a seaport quarantine office within the department to take over all the functions and powers of the abolished seaport quarantine administration, and to establish a Chinese Medicine Committee within the department with one director and five to nine members appointed by the Department of Health from those with knowledge of Chinese medicine. When the Yuan meeting discussed the case, Peng Yangguang, Liu Tong, Lu Zhiyi, and others advocated adding a deputy director-general to the department to position Chinese medicine talents and promote the integration of Chinese and Western medicine. Some legislators strongly opposed it, which led to a debate about the merits of Chinese and Western medicine. After a vote, only eight people agreed, and it was not passed. Later, when the name and functions of the newly established agency for managing Chinese medicine in the department were discussed, the committee members had disputes again. Later, according to the chairman's motion, the name of the agency was changed to the Chinese Medicine Committee, and its functions were changed to handle matters related to Chinese medicine. The main point of the amended Chinese Medicine Ordinance is to change the agency that reviews the qualifications of Chinese medicine practitioners from the original "Ministry of Interior" to the "Chinese Medicine Committee of the Department of Health." (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Gambling Den Cracked Down in Tianjin Japanese Concession

(Tianjin) At midnight on the 3rd, the roulette gambling den set up by Koreans and Russians in the Japanese concession was surrounded by Japanese police, and 79 Chinese gamblers, 4 Russians, and 3 Koreans were arrested. The owner of the gambling den, Liu Baozhen, escaped. Among the arrested criminals, there were several field commanders and provincial governors. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

Japan Plans to Monopolize Salt Industry in North China

(Tianjin) For the second batch of reed salt exports, the Japanese side plans to form the North China Salt Industry Company with the Xingzhong Company as the mainstay, build warehouses and factories in the salt marshes occupied in Tanggu and Dagang, implement chemical methods for export, and directly contact various marsh merchants for purchase, with a planned volume of 200,000 to 300,000 tons. This matter damages our salt affairs. The Changlu Salt Administration telegraphed the Ministry of Finance on the 4th for instructions, and various marsh merchants also telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to report and request a ban. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

Preparatory Committee of the National Goods Joint Venture Company Holds Inaugural Meeting, Wu Dingchang Presides and Delivers Opening Remarks

(Nanjing) The Preparatory Committee of the National Goods Joint Venture Company held its inaugural meeting at the Ministry of Industry at 3 PM on the afternoon of the 4th. More than ten people including Weng Wenhao, Wu Dingchang, Zhou Zhichun, Wang Xiaolai, Liu Hongsheng, Hu Xiyuan, Fang Yexian, Qian Xinzhi, Huang Yanpei, Wang Xingyao, and Pan Yangyao attended. Wu Dingchang presided and delivered the opening remarks. He first stated that Chairman Jiang believes that the National Economic Movement is the new life of the Chinese nation and his lifelong career. Therefore, in addition to being involved in politics and military affairs, the Chairman still devotes most of his energy and time to economic construction and strives for progress. Even during his inspection tours in various provinces, he continuously telegraphed to urge us, which made us very excited and dared not to slack off. He hoped that the gentlemen in the industrial and commercial circles and the financial circles would understand the Chairman's good intentions and work together to help the General Economic Construction Association. He then stated the significance of the General Economic Construction Association's advocacy of establishing a National Goods Joint Transportation Company and explained two points: (1) The purpose of the government in organizing this company is to seek benefits for national goods throughout the country, not to develop national goods in one place. Its nature is very universal. In terms of categories, it includes machine-woven products, handicrafts, and local products. (2) In terms of machine-made products, it is not limited to machine-woven products in Shanghai. Machine-woven products from all over the country are also being collected. Therefore, its source is not limited to products from a certain place, nor is it specifically for the development of any factory or company. Therefore, the government has four key points when initiating the National Goods Joint Venture Company, which it hopes will be noted: A. When the company raises capital, all national goods companies and factories across the country will be given the same opportunity to invest so that they can participate. Therefore, the method of publicly soliciting funds is adopted. When the shares needed by the company and factory are insufficient to control, the government can transfer them. The government intends to promote and will never compete with the people for profits. B. After the National Goods Joint Venture Company is established, no matter where or which factory produces the goods, as long as the goods are fairly determined by the government agency to be needed by the people, they will have the opportunity to wholesale and sell within the company's scope. The same treatment will be given to national handicrafts and local products. C. The identification of all national goods must be accurate, and the price of the goods must be fair. The government will strictly supervise these two points to prevent consumers from being deceived. D. Department stores or vendors outside the scope of the joint venture company will be allowed to sell national goods by the National Goods Joint Venture Company at wholesale prices, and they will never be deprived of the opportunity to sell. The establishment of this company is to systematically promote the sales of national goods and has no intention of monopolizing the market. The government will never allow it to become a monopolistic business. Finally, he hoped that all national goods factories, national goods companies, and other people in the industrial, commercial, and financial sectors would help with the progress with the spirit of seeking the public good for the benefit of the masses and sacrificing individual private interests. After Wu finished his opening remarks, he continued to report on the purpose and process of the preparatory work. Subsequently, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Yanpei, Wu Yun, Chu, and Zhang Yiou successively delivered speeches, contributing many opinions on the preparatory matters. Finally, Wu Dingchang delivered a speech, hoping that the committee members would provide more comments so that the company could be prepared perfectly and the business could develop rapidly. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM. In the evening, Wu Dingchang hosted a banquet for all the attendees. The atmosphere was extremely pleasant, and they dispersed. In addition, fifty factories including the Family Industry Cooperative sent representatives such as Li Xinpu to petition the Ministry of Industry to expand the organization of the National Goods Joint Venture Company to popularize it. It is said that the result was very satisfactory. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Central Government Unifies Foreign Affairs Authority, and Three Methods of Joint Ventures Between China and Foreign Countries, The National Government Reissues Orders to the Executive Yuan to Instruct Compliance

(Nanjing) The National Government instructed the Executive Yuan on the 4th: In order to comply with the matter, according to the decision of the 171st meeting of the Central Political Conference on January 16 of the 18th year, all foreign affairs negotiations by the provinces should be handled by the central government. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs should notify both China and foreign countries that no matter what agreement is signed between any country and the provincial officials, the central government cannot recognize its validity. On April 9 of the 19th year, the 222nd meeting of the Central Political Conference also discussed three methods for utilizing foreign capital: (1) Investment method, (2) Franchise method, (3) Loan method. The central government has already made clear regulations on unifying foreign affairs authority and methods for joint ventures between China and foreign countries, and officials of all provinces and cities should abide by them. Recently, there have been discussions about foreign affairs events and joint ventures between China and foreign countries in various provinces and cities. The 26th meeting of the Central Political Committee on November 19 of this year decided to reissue the previous order. Therefore, it is hereby reissued that all foreign affairs negotiations by provinces and cities and clauses on joint ventures with foreigners are invalid unless approved by the central government. It is instructed to comply in order to show solemnity and maintain national rights. This order. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Wang Jun's Coffin Arrives in Nanjing, He Yingqin and Others Go to Pukou to Greet and Offer Sacrifices, Zhu Peide Presides Over the Sacrifice and Tears Fall

(Nanjing) Wang Jun's coffin was transported from the front line to Nanjing at 4 AM on the morning of the 4th. More than a thousand people, including Wang's comrades-in-arms, relatives, friends, and fellow villagers from Yunnan, gathered at the Zhongshan Wharf in Xiaguan, then crossed the river to Pukou to greet and offer sacrifices. Central Committee members who personally greeted were He Yingqin, Cheng Qian, Zhu Peide, Gu Zhenglun, Ma Chaojun, Li Liejun, Zhang Lisheng, etc. After the coffin arrived at the station, the whole group greeted and offered sacrifices at the station. After crossing the river, they offered sacrifices again at the Zhongshan Wharf in Xiaguan and then escorted it to the First Park for burial. Zhu Peide presided over the sacrifice. During the sacrifice, Zhu wept sadly, and everyone present was solemn and moved, expressing their grief. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Manager of Xuchang Tobacco Company Assassinated

(Hankou) A telegram received here today states that Mr. Newson, an American and advisor to the Nanjing government, as well as the manager of the government-run Xuchang Tobacco Company, was assassinated in Xuchang, Henan Province, by an unknown assailant. Mr. Newson was a native of Salisbury, North Carolina, USA, and was 40 years old. His wife and 11-year-old daughter are currently in Hankou. Yesterday, the first telegram only mentioned that Mr. Newson was seriously injured in the assassination. A certain famous doctor here and the manager of the British American Tobacco Company immediately prepared to take the plane borrowed from Mr. Zhang Xueliang to Xuchang this morning. However, before they could depart, the tragic news of Mr. Newson's death had already reached here. The motive for Mr. Newson's murder is unknown, but it is said that Mr. Newson had received multiple threatening letters before his death. It is also said that Mr. Wu Tingsheng, the Chinese manager of the Xuchang Tobacco Company, was also assassinated in Xuchang last year. At that time, the general opinion was that the motive of the murderer was mostly resentment towards the official operation of the tobacco business. It is heard that Mr. Newson has a brother who is doing business in Shanghai, and it is said that Mr. Newson's body will be transported to Hankou soon. At the same time, the US Consulate is investigating the case. Mr. Newson's mother is currently in her hometown. (Reuters dispatch on the 4th)

Sai Jinhua Passed Away Yesterday, A Generation of Beauty Ends Like This, To Be Buried Next to Parrot Tomb

(Beiping) Sai Jinhua passed away at 2:30 AM on the morning of the 4th. Her funeral is extremely desolate. The gentry of Beiping have launched a fundraising campaign and decided to bury her next to the Parrot Tomb in Taoranting, Beiping, for future generations to mourn. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

(Beiping) Sai Jinhua, who lived in seclusion in the ancient capital and was famous throughout the country, passed away at approximately 4 AM on the morning of the 4th, at the age of 62. Her funeral was desolate, and only with the help of friends was she able to be hastily buried. It is tragic that a generation of beauty ended like this. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Audience with Mongolian and Tibetan Political and Religious Leaders Postponed

(Nanjing) The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission originally planned to summon Mongolian and Tibetan political and religious leaders to Beijing on the 20th of this month to facilitate communication between the central government and the border areas. However, this move has now been decided to be postponed to next year. According to the person in charge of the commission, the reason for the postponement is that those who were summoned to Beijing this time included dozens of League and Banner leaders and religious leaders from Suiyuan and Qinghai provinces. Currently, banditry is rampant in Suiyuan Province, and the League and Banner leaders are responsible for maintaining local security and protecting their territory. Therefore, they cannot spare the time. Moreover, the date of the audience is relatively hurried, and some remote provinces may not be able to arrive in time. Therefore, due to these various practical difficulties, it has been decided to postpone it to next year, and the exact date has not been determined. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Hubei's Preventive Measures Against Labor Unrest

(Hankou) The provincial capital's agencies are deeply concerned that small groups may instigate labor unrest or sabotage due to the presence of numerous factories and workers in Wuchang. On the 4th, they convened meetings with various factory and labor unions to discuss preventive measures against labor unrest. The measures will be announced and implemented after being approved by higher authorities. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

Continued Drop in River Water Levels Leads to Increased Freight Charges

(Hankou) The water level of the Yangtze River is unusually shallow this year. The Hankou Merchants Steam Navigation Company has been charging a shallow water fee of 25% for various water-land joint transportation goods since the 1st. Due to the continued and rapid drop in the river water level, the Merchants Steam Navigation Company has stipulated that starting from the 10th, except for general merchandise, which will temporarily be charged an additional 25%, other goods will be charged an additional 50%. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Fire Breaks Out in the Rear Building of the Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters

(Nanjing) At 3:20 PM on the afternoon of the 4th, a fire broke out in the rear building of the Nanjing Municipal Party Headquarters, destroying the entire upper floor and part of the lower floor. The files were all rescued, and only a portion was lost. The household survey materials and the bound volumes of the Nanjing and Shanghai newspapers were burned. The cause of the fire is being investigated. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

Liu Xiang Requests Leave to Return to His Hometown to Recuperate

(Chengdu) Liu Xiang telegraphed Chairman Jiang on the 4th, requesting a ten-day leave to return to his hometown of Dayi to recuperate. The duties of the provincial government were handed over to Secretary-General Deng Hanxiang, and the duties of the governor's office were temporarily taken over by Chief of Staff Fu Chang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Committee members Xu Enzeng, Gao Tingzi, Zhao Zukang, Song Xishang, etc., attended. The following were approved: (A) Appointing committee members to draft a plan for the overall planning and adjustment of the national transportation network. (B) Methods for expanding the railway sector, improving technology, and reorganizing personnel were also assigned to committee members to draft. (C) Appointing personnel to draft methods for improving engineering in the highway sector and methods for utilizing existing highways. (D) Appointing personnel to draft methods for developing shipping in the shipping sector, improving sailing and management methods, and recovering navigation rights. (E) Appointing personnel to draft methods for postal and telecommunications liaison with transportation in the postal and telecommunications sector. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Xinpu Guanyun: A young girl, Ma Xiulan, committed suicide by throwing herself into Xinpu in anger at the bandits invading Suiyuan, unable to kill the enemy. (Special dispatch on the 4th)

Current Commentary

The Seriousness of the Qingdao Incident

— All

At a time when the beacons of war on the border were urgently signaling danger, the scenic city of Qingdao unexpectedly stirred up unwarranted storms. Over a thousand Japanese naval landing troops, fully armed, disembarked and densely deployed to various positions, surrounding Party and police institutions, searching for books and documents, and even beating and insulting staff, and indiscriminately arresting people. They cut off communication lines and acted with unrestrained impunity. Although those arrested were soon released, groups of Japanese soldiers remained in the city, carrying out patrol duties. Such excessive behavior by the military of a friendly nation is not only shocking to the people of our country, but also astonishing to the world. The future course of events is difficult to predict, and the increasingly fragile friendship between China and Japan has once again suffered an unexpected blow, creating an even more tense situation. This is an undeniable fact clearly evident at present.

The root of this incident lies in the Japanese side using the pretext of worsening labor unrest to take decisive measures. However, according to the facts, the opposite is true. It is found that there are nine textile factories established by Japanese merchants in Qingdao. Recently, workers at three factories, including Dakang, engaged in slowdowns to demand wage increases. After repeated mediation by local government officials, there was a possibility of calming the situation. However, the factory owners suddenly convened a meeting the day before yesterday and unanimously decided to shut down all factories. Even the six factories that did not participate in the slowdown, such as Gongda Cang Kou, were also completely closed. On one hand, 30,000 laborers were suddenly thrown into unemployment, while on the other, warships were dispatched and troops were sent, deliberately creating panic. Everyone knows what Ma Zhao is up to. Otherwise, with the trivial matter of labor disputes, a common occurrence in society, it would not be difficult to achieve peace if sincerity were shown. Why engage in suspicion and speculation, turning it into an unresolvable situation? Even if, as the Japanese side claims, they feel unable to manage the businesses, they still have appropriate steps to take and the need to respond separately. Why close down all six factories that did not participate in the labor unrest? And why resort to illegal military means to create an unfathomable situation? Foreign dispatches claim that the arrival of Japanese military officer Major Yazaki in Qingdao is related to this military action. Understanding the truth, one can see the implications of this.

Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie protested to the Japanese consul after the incident occurred, and Foreign Minister Zhang Qun also raised three demands when meeting with Ambassador Kawagoe. The progress of subsequent negotiations is being watched by the general public. One point we must especially emphasize is that in our own territory, we are suddenly subjected to the trampling of foreign troops; the Party headquarters, the repository of our dignity, is subjected to encirclement and search by foreign soldiers; and the leaders of our respected institutions are subjected to unwarranted and illegal arrest. What then is the meaning of national sovereignty? Even if the negotiations result in the withdrawal of Japanese troops and the return of documents, how can we tolerate and gloss over this act of infringing upon our sovereignty? After the spokesperson of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs repeatedly stated the determination to defend territorial sovereignty, this blatant act of infringing upon our sovereignty occurred. The grief and indignation of the authorities are self-evident. In order to implement their claims, what means will they use to exert their greatest efforts?

British King Fights for Freedom of Marriage: Prefers to Sacrifice the Throne for Love Rather Than Compromise; Various Parties Plead to Change His Mind; Mrs. Simpson Quietly Leaves England for France

(London) According to the Daily Mail, despite the entreaties of the cabinet and autonomous governments, the British King remains unmoved. The King insists that this matter is difficult to compromise. If he decides to abdicate, he will announce it to Parliament. The Daily Mail also learned that the King's lover, Mrs. Simpson, plans to travel to Paris this morning on the King's private plane. (December 4th, Reuters)

(London) The cabinet convened a special meeting of the House of Commons today to discuss King Edward VIII's marriage to Mrs. Simpson. However, both the government and the public have effectively given up hope of dissuading Edward from abdicating. At 9:00 this morning, the King returned to London from Belverdere Fortress, but at the same time, a truck loaded with luggage departed from the fortress. (December 4th, Guomin News)

(London) Regarding the wedding issue, well-informed sources recently stated that after the King discussed the matter with Queen Mary, his brothers the Duke of York, the Duke of Gloucester, and the Duke of Kent yesterday, he is now considering a compromise that would prevent the abdication from occurring. (December 4th, Havas News)

(London) King Edward VIII, after conferring with Queen Mary, his brothers the Duke of York, and Prime Minister Baldwin yesterday, abdication is inevitable unless there are unexpected changes. Regarding this matter, political figures recently stated that the King's decision will be announced in Parliament next Monday. Therefore, the King theoretically has three days to carefully consider and change his mind. Some members of Parliament also hope that the King can cancel his original decision. However, semi-official sources believe that the King has already made up his mind and does not intend to change it, and the abdication could be announced today, but it is delayed because the succession issue has not been completely resolved. Well-informed sources also stated that the courtiers originally hoped that the King could change his mind after Queen Mary's earnest persuasion, but the King, due to the scandalous private affairs causing public uproar and damaging the dignity of the monarch, has already decided to abdicate, and he made this clear when he met with Prime Minister Baldwin. (December 4th, Havas News)

(London) It was learned from reliable sources today that if the government does not compromise on King Edward's marriage, Edward has decided to abdicate within 48 hours. Although this news has not been confirmed, Edward spoke briefly with the Duke of York at Buckingham Palace at 8:00 this evening, and then together they went to Marlborough House to visit Queen Mary. It is said that the King plans to meet with the cabinet and the Privy Council tomorrow to announce his final decision. It is reported that Prime Minister Baldwin informed the King that if Mrs. Simpson does not leave England, the cabinet will resign. The King was furious upon hearing this and made the decision to abdicate. It was later learned that Mrs. Simpson may depart for France, and Edward may also abdicate to follow her. Baldwin also told the King that he has the support of the Labor Party and that if the King does not heed the cabinet's advice, he will not be able to form a government. (December 3rd, Guomin News)

(Paris) It is learned here that Mrs. Simpson arrived in Rouen from London at 3:30 this morning and then came to Paris before 11:30. It is said that Mrs. Simpson will go to Versailles to visit an American friend. (December 4th, Reuters)

(Paris) Mrs. Simpson arrived at the Petit Trianon in Versailles this afternoon. When Mrs. Simpson left Dieppe at 2:50 this morning, she was accompanied by several plainclothes detectives. (December 4th, Reuters)

British Prime Minister Announces No Intention to Create Legislation: Obtains the Consent of the Entire Federation; There Is No Precedent for Unequal Marriage

(London) This afternoon, British Prime Minister Baldwin announced in the House of Commons that the government is not prepared to introduce legislation to facilitate the marriage proposed by the British King. The issue currently being discussed is a matter of common concern to the entire federation. Without the consent of all autonomous dominions, this change cannot take effect. Baldwin also stated that he was very satisfied with the results of his inquiries to all parties because there was no indication of consent to this matter. Baldwin added, "I feel it is very appropriate to make this statement before adjourning today, because this can dispel misunderstandings. I have no other comments to make at this time." Baldwin also replied to a question from Labor opposition leader Attlee, stating that some newspapers have argued that if the British King insists on marrying Mrs. Simpson, her title does not necessarily have to be Queen. This concept has no constitutional basis whatsoever. There is no precedent in British law for such an unequal marriage. The Royal Marriages Act of 1772 does not apply to the British King himself, but only stipulates that the marriages of other members of the royal family are not valid without the King's permission. This law has nothing to do with the current matter. The British King does not need to obtain the permission of any other authority, but the woman he marries must nominally be called Queen. The only way to avoid this outcome is to create a separate law for this special event, but the government is not prepared to propose this method. And if there is to be any reform, it must take effect after the autonomous dominions agree. Baldwin finished speaking and then adjourned the meeting. (December 4th, Reuters)

Discussions in the Palace: Queen Mother Reveals Unhappiness; Brothers Also Offer Advice

(London) The Duke of York, the heir to the throne, turned back on his way to Edinburgh and arrived in London yesterday morning, visiting the Queen Mother and having dinner with her, accompanied by his wife. The Duke of York, his younger brother the Duke of Kent, and his uncle Earl of Athlone all canceled all public appointments yesterday.

Last night, after the British King visited the Queen Mother and returned to Buckingham Palace, the Duke of York came to visit, and the brothers had a long talk. At 1:30 this morning, the British King went to Belverdere Fortress and planned to return to London before noon. Before leaving, the Prime Minister conferred with the Department of Autonomous Dominions and then entered the palace to pay his respects. The Prime Minister spent the whole day advising and, after leaving the palace, returned to his residence on Downing Street to rest. Queen Mary took time yesterday to take a car to Sidingham to see the ruins of the burned-down Crystal Palace.

(London) It is reported that Queen Mary has directly or indirectly expressed to the King her disapproval of his relationship with Mrs. Simpson. The Duke of York also offered much advice when he visited the Queen Mother today. The King earnestly pleaded with the Queen Mother, but she was very displeased at the time. (December 3rd, Guomin News)

(London) After the King visited the Queen Mother with the Duke of York today, he returned to Buckingham Palace. It is rumored that the Queen Mother and Princess Mary wept together after the King left. (December 3rd, Guomin News)

Constitutional Disputes Emerge: The British Empire Reveals Its True Intentions; Prime Minister Runs Around to Mediate, Looking Worried; Autonomous Dominions Are Willing to Support the Government

(London) According to well-informed sources, the situation caused by the constitutional dispute has greatly eased after the British King conferred with the Queen Mother, his brothers, and Prime Minister Baldwin last night. It is generally believed that a compromise proposal acceptable to all relevant parties, including the British King, the Cabinet, and the governments of the autonomous dominions, is currently being considered. The nature of this proposal has not yet been disclosed. When the House of Commons reconvened at 11:00 this morning, the Prime Minister was unwilling to disclose anything about the issue. The Prime Minister, in a tired tone and with a pale and worried face, answered questions from opposition leader Attlee, saying that he had nothing to report at this time. Attlee also asked when the truth about this matter could be disclosed to the public. The Prime Minister replied that he knew that the House of Commons was very concerned about this matter and eager to know the truth, but he could not continue to speak at the moment. The House of Lords also met at 11:00 this morning, but adjourned after just over a minute. Before the House of Commons convened today, cabinet members had been meeting for two hours, and they will continue to meet in the afternoon, as all cabinet members have canceled their daytime affairs. The British King slept for four hours at Belverdere Fortress, rising early in the morning. He did not take his usual morning walk in the garden. In the morning, his brother the Duke of York drove to Marlborough House to confer with the Queen Mother. The Duke's private secretary also visited the Prime Minister at 10 Downing Street. (December 4th, Reuters)

(London) The Empire and the domestic government now believe that the British King's marriage has reached the point of "revealing the dagger after the map has been unrolled." The British King must either give up Mrs. Simpson or abdicate, one or the other. It is generally believed that the governments of the dominions are firmly supporting the domestic government's opinion, having resolutely stated that the autonomous dominions of the Empire do not approve of the current marriage. Telegrams between London and the capitals of the autonomous dominions are constantly being exchanged. It is expected that a concrete decision will be made in one or two days. The Cabinet, Buckingham Palace, and Marlborough House, where Queen Mary resides, were busy until after midnight last night. Prime Minister Baldwin entered Buckingham Palace at 9:15 last night to pay his respects to the British King, leaving after 55 minutes. At 10:40, the British King drove to Marlborough House to see his mother, returning to the palace 40 minutes later. At the same time, the Prime Minister went to the House of Commons to confer with Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, Secretary of State for Dominion Affairs MacDonald, High Commissioner for the Union of South Africa in London Walters, and High Commissioner for Canada in London Massey. At 10:40, the Prime Minister left the House of Commons. Twenty minutes later, MacDonald, Walters, and Massey went to the Department of Autonomous Dominions to continue their discussions. Walters and Massey said goodbye to MacDonald at 11:40, both saying they had no comments to make and would return to their residences. MacDonald left the Department of Autonomous Dominions at ten minutes after midnight.

The House of Commons adjourned at 7:55 last night, completing its routine business three hours earlier than usual due to the constitutional dispute. Both Houses convened at 11:00 this morning.

It is reported that the autonomous dominions are now exercising their rights under the Statute of Westminster, and any issue they believe involves autonomy will be directly presented to the British King. Their telegrams to the domestic government express firm opinions, so the British King must now deal not only with his cabinet, but also with the various groups representing the opinions of the governments within the Empire. The opinions expressed by the autonomous dominions reflect their deep concern about the fact that the United States has not suppressed the coverage of the news, fearing that this will continue to affect the entire Empire.

It is generally believed that the domestic government may not create legislation to allow for a compromise marriage, even if there is a legal possibility. Cabinet members clearly cannot force the King to abandon his lover or implement abdication, and the King can dismiss cabinet members or the cabinet can resign to express their dissatisfaction. However, in the current situation, it is difficult to find suitable candidates to replace the cabinet after resignation, so for the sake of the country and the Empire, neither dismissal nor resignation seems likely to occur.

Because the autonomous dominions are directly concerned about this matter, the opinions expressed in their telegrams must be taken into account. Therefore, the government will need at least a day or two to make a final decision.

Yesterday, crowds gathered near Buckingham Palace and the Prime Minister's residence on Downing Street, standing for a long time, demonstrating the people's concern about this matter. All newspapers reported on the Prime Minister's meeting with opposition leader Attlee and the London-based commissioners for the autonomous dominions. Everyone is paying attention to these discussions. (December 4th, Reuters)

British House of Commons: Discusses the Wedding Issue; Even Without a Royal Mandate to Preside Over the Ceremony, Parliament Should Still Swear Allegiance to the King - Startling Motion by Opposition Member -

(London) When the House of Commons met this afternoon, opposition Labor leader Major Attlee questioned Prime Minister Baldwin about the King's wedding issue. The chamber was full, but it was solemn and silent. Major Attlee often said, "Has a constitutional difficulty arisen? Will the Prime Minister make an official statement today?" The Prime Minister immediately withdrew for a few minutes, and when he returned to his seat, his face was pale. He replied, "I do not intend to make any statement at this time. As for the so-called constitutional difficulty, it does not currently exist. In such a situation, it is inappropriate for you to ask me questions." Extreme Conservative leader Churchill then rose to speak, saying, "Can the Prime Minister provide us with assurances that there will be no irreversible actions before a formal statement is made to Parliament?" The Prime Minister replied, "I will consider Mr. Churchill's question, but that is all I will say at this time." Major Attlee continued to ask, "People are currently in a state of panic. Can the Prime Minister assure the House of Commons that a statement will be made as soon as possible?" The Prime Minister replied that this request would be considered. (December 3rd, Havas News)

Then former cabinet member Colonel Wedgwood (former Liberal member of the House of Commons, now independent, sitting in the opposition seats) proposed a motion in the House of Commons, stating that the oath of allegiance to the British King is not affected by any form of coronation ceremony or the absence of any dignitaries at the coronation. The House of Commons must not support anyone else as British King. The members of the House of Commons were greatly bewildered by this motion. Reuters learned that the "absence of any dignitaries" referred to by Wedgwood was referring to the Archbishop of Canterbury, the Bishop of Bradford, the Prime Minister, and other figures. Wedgwood told a Reuters reporter that the religious ceremony of coronation is merely a church tradition, and is not related to the British people other than the willingness to maintain customary practices. In any case, a King must be a King, and all costs must be spared to avoid the realization of abdication. (December 3rd, Reuters)

Wedgwood also stated that in any case, the act of abdication must be avoided at all costs, because "the current King is extremely popular with the people, and any change in the throne could plunge the country into a state of division. If the House of Commons were to hold a general election to solicit public opinion on the abdication issue, the result would be that the people would also be attached to the King. In short, this issue should not be decided solely by the cabinet, but should be decided by the entire Parliament, as was the case with Richard II." (Note: Richard II was born in 1367 and died in 1400, and abdicated in 1399) (December 3rd, Reuters)

Hold a General Election to Test Public Opinion: Wedgwood's Proposal Resonates with Various Parties

(London) As soon as the news of Wedgwood's motion in the House of Commons was broadcast, Wedgwood received 50 letters and telegrams in an instant, supporting his opinion that all costs should be spared to avoid the realization of the British King's abdication, and advocating holding a general election to seek national support for the British King. (December 3rd, Reuters)

London Public Opinion: Filled with Enthusiasm for Support: Commoner Marriage Does Not Violate Tradition: Hope to Find a Proper Solution to Prevent Abdication from Occurring

(London) Today, The Times published an editorial explaining its opposition to the marriage of the British King and Mrs. Simpson, stating that we must not misunderstand the nature of the opposition to the marriage proposed by the British King. It is important to know that the root cause of the opposition has been carefully reported by foreign newspapers and repeatedly expressed by domestic public opinion, all of which believe that it is due to a long-standing custom that the King should not marry a commoner or an American woman. If the British King can win the love of one of his citizens, then the whole country will share his happiness, and from the daughters of most American people, he may gain the same approval and marry them. However, there is a major obstacle to the marriage proposed by the British King this time, that is, the woman whom the King intends to marry has been divorced twice, and both of her former husbands are still alive.

The newspaper also stated that there is a general impression in Britain that the British King has informed the cabinet of his intention to marry, and the cabinet members have interfered with the British King's choice of spouse by objecting to it. According to the newspaper's parliamentary reporter today, the truth of the matter is that the British King has indicated that he intends to conclude a marriage that requires a special act of Parliament to pass, and he has first inquired whether this matter can be passed, and the cabinet ministers have all replied that it is impossible. Therefore, the theory that cabinet members interfered in the British King's private affairs is difficult to defend.

(London) The British newspapers' criticism of the British King's marriage remains very moderate, and they are full of enthusiastic love and sympathy for the King himself. Today, several widely circulated newspapers in Britain have gradually expressed their unwillingness to see the British King announce his abdication. For example, the Daily Mail contained a piece of news stating that more than 7,000 people gathered at Albert Hall last night, enthusiastically chanting "Long live the British King" and singing the national anthem. According to the newspaper, abdication is not a question, because the possible harms of this matter are limitless and will greatly affect the British Empire. Therefore, the federal nation, at this time of unprecedented global crisis, cannot abandon this King rich in talent and knowledge. The newspaper also said, "Abdication will not occur. The British King and the cabinet must find a way to resolve this matter. The people need their monarch, because the current King serves the Empire with loyalty and enthusiasm, and the national sentiment is extremely supportive of him." The Daily Express asked in its editorial, "Are we willing to lose the current King or retain him?" The answer is not difficult to see in the people's expressions. The News Chronicle said that there are now various signs that the public's sympathy for the British King is growing, and they feel that the King's abdication will cause misfortune. If there is a solution that both the British King and the cabinet can accept, the British people will feel very gratified. If the Empire loses its beloved King due to hasty decisions, the country will suffer a loss, which goes without saying. (December 4th, Reuters)

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies is scheduled to debate the government's foreign policy starting this Friday. Therefore, Delbos decided to issue an official statement in the Chamber of Deputies to respond to Eden's speech and express that France is willing to bear the obligations stipulated in the Locarno Treaty with Britain. As for the Spanish situation, France will consistently support the non-intervention policy. Japanese Naval Landing Party Lands Armed in Qingdao, Posts Abound, Like Facing a Major Enemy, Searching Party Headquarters and Arresting Many People

Qingdao News, the workers of various Japanese-owned textile factories in this city once went on strike to demand improved treatment from the factories. The city authorities have tried their best to mediate, and the factories have resumed operations one after another. Unexpectedly, the factories refused to fulfill the terms of the agreement and dismissed more than three people without cause, which further provoked a labor unrest. Factories such as Dakang, Nei Wai Mian, and Longxing also went on strike one after another. In order to preemptively strike, the factories jointly decided at noon on the 2nd of this month to suddenly close all six other factories that did not participate in the strike, causing tens of thousands of workers to lose their jobs overnight and creating an unstable situation in the market. The factories also requested the Navy to send nine warships to patrol the front and rear seas to demonstrate, citing the protection of factories and expatriates. At around 3:00 AM on the 3rd of this month, more than a thousand naval landing party members suddenly landed armed, and rushed to the areas around the country's factories in Dongzhen, Sifang, and Cangku, posting abudant positions like facing a major enemy. They also sent teams to occupy various key points to cut off traffic. They then went to the city party headquarters, the Jiaoji Railway Party Headquarters, the National Martial Arts Hall, the First Section of the Jiaoji Railway Police, the Municipal Library, and the Pingmin Daily News, searching each one, and arrested nine people including Xiang Zongding, secretary of the National Martial Arts Hall, and Zhang Legu, editor of the Pingmin Daily News, and detained them at the Japanese Naval Assembly Hall on Diping Road for strict interrogation. It is said that the reason for the arrest of Xiang and Zhang was that they had launched a patriotic movement and donated funds to support Suiyuan. The Japanese side believes that this labor unrest was incited by the patriotic movement. When the Japanese army carried out the search, they also confiscated all the guns and ammunition of a part of the Public Security Bureau's security team and the First Section of the Jiaoji Railway Police, but returned the guns and ammunition immediately afterwards. After receiving the report, the city government was led by Mayor Shen Honglie to convene the heads of the various bureaus to discuss countermeasures. On one hand, they telegraphed the central government to report the situation of the Japanese Navy landing in Qingdao and requested instructions on everything. On the other hand, they made a serious protest with the Japanese consulate and the Navy. The Japanese army also knew that they were in the wrong and released the arrested people at the same time. At 12:30 PM, the Public Security Bureau sent police to bring back the arrested people. Mayor Shen personally consoled the arrested people. In the afternoon, the Japanese Marine Corps began to return to the ships one after another, but the Japanese troops stationed in the factories remained on guard at each factory. They also dispatched armed patrol teams to patrol the city from time to time, and the citizens avoided them. However, the order of the city remains normal, and there are no changes at present. According to Mr. Zhang, who was arrested, when he was released, the Japanese military authorities strictly instructed that newspapers are not allowed to publish any news about anti-Japanese and patriotic movements in the future, otherwise they will be dealt with by military law.

Tensions in Suiyuan, Hebei Province's Aid-Sui Movement is Enthusiastic, Education Sector Takes the Lead in Unanimous Response, Farmers and Merchants Follow Suit and Actively Contribute

Baoding Correspondence: Since the situation in Suiyuan became critical, our troops fighting bandits on the front lines have been winning victories in the frozen wasteland, and have recently bravely recovered Bailingmiao, which has inspired the entire nation. Recently, the matter of sending supplies and comforting the troops has swept the country like a storm, and the enthusiastic emotions have reached a boiling point. Hebei Province is located in the gateway to North China, and although it is currently still in a state of temporary peace, the future evolution is also of great importance. Therefore, the inspiring atmosphere of the people of this province is extremely profound. Starting from Baoding, where the provincial capital is located, to the counties, villages, and towns, they have launched an aid-Sui movement, actively sending supplies. All official and private schools have begun to organize various forms of aid-Sui movement. As for official propaganda lectures and street fundraising, in order to maintain public order and respect the wishes of the local authorities, they are generally not carried out. Although the surface is very quiet, the enthusiastic spirit of the people has indeed penetrated the lower levels. Therefore, in recent decades, the education sector in Hebei Province has taken the lead in launching the "Donate One Day's Income to Contribute to the Government" campaign. The Baoding Colleges and Museums Federation took the lead by example, donating 2,500 yuan and sending a condolence delegation to Suiyuan to comfort the troops. Zhao County, Renqiu, Xincheng, Qingyuan, and other counties have responded one after another and donated money successively. The Hebei Provincial Medical College has also organized a medical team, providing its own medicines to set off to the front. The Provincial Women's Normal School has also recently held a large-scale fundraising entertainment fair to raise large sums of money to purchase woolen cloth, foreign leather, etc., and personally rush to make fur sets for the soldiers fighting the enemy, so as to send them to the front to keep out the cold. In addition to doing their best to raise funds, all the teachers and students of Baoding Middle School have also set out on different routes, going deep into the rural suburbs and persuading merchants and farmers. They have achieved great success in recent days. Therefore, in addition to the education sector unanimously conducting the aid-Sui movement in Hebei Province, farmers, merchants, and even vendors in other counties have also followed suit and are increasing day by day. There are many people who donate one or two yuan, or even one or two dimes, or even two or three cents. Some ordinary citizens only know to donate money to comfort the troops, but do not know where to donate, so there are many people who ask the police where to donate. This kind of enthusiastic emotion is enough to make us feel extremely excited and gratified. (2nd) There are more and more unemployed people. If they lack food, they will inevitably take risks. Local security is worrying. It is reported that Guangdong Province relies on Annam and Siam for its food supply. In the past, foreign rice imports were not taxed, because food is the most important thing for the people. If there is surplus food in the market, it can be expected that every family will have enough to eat. Even in recent times, when the customs levies taxes, it is feared that foreign rice will be dumped, which will hurt farmers and hinder their livelihoods. The tax rate on foreign rice is inherently elastic, and can be adjusted according to the situation to regulate the market. Now, Guangdong Province has suffered from summer floods and autumn droughts, and a famine is imminent. The price of rice is also rising, and there is a trend of continued increase. The people are complaining and the situation is dangerous. Han Mou and Mu Song have repeatedly discussed that it is impossible to provide relief without suppressing the price of rice. Moreover, the winter defense is tight, and the people are poor and prone to theft. It is estimated that there will be another half year before the next harvest, so it is urgently necessary to stabilize the price of rice to alleviate the people's difficulties. It is proposed that the central government should consider the famine in Guangdong Province and the difficulty of the people's food supply, and order the Guangdong Customs to temporarily exempt foreign rice imports from taxes from the date of the order until the end of July 26, in order to reduce costs and gradually stabilize the price of rice. Once the early rice is harvested next year and the harvest is abundant, the taxes can be reinstated. The people of Guangdong will be deeply grateful. In addition to submitting a report to the Executive Yuan and a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, we jointly request your review and implementation.

Guangdong Province is Suffering from Famine and the Price of Rice is Extremely High, Authorities Appeal to the Central Government to Temporarily Remove the Foreign Rice Tax to Stabilize the Price of Rice and Relieve the Current Distress of the People

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has recently suffered a poor late rice harvest, and the domestic supply of food is insufficient. The import of foreign rice has been cut off due to excessive taxation. In this transition period, the price of rice is high and rises several times a day. Currently, one yuan can only buy six or seven catties of brown rice, and the lives of ordinary people are difficult. The lower classes are working hard all day long, and are sighing "have food but no place to live" or "have a place to live but no food to eat." This is because there are many unemployed people in the society, and the people are about to take risks. The future of public security is truly unbearable. The Rice Industry Association has previously strongly advocated the abolition of the foreign rice import tax in order to regulate the grain supply and prevent the interruption of the source, which is a symptomatic treatment for stabilizing the price of rice. After this proposal was launched, the provincial government and the Department of Finance also considered it feasible. They convened several studies by financial experts and decided to maintain the food supply. On the one hand, they negotiated with Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces to transport rice to Guangdong. On the other hand, they decided to ask the central authorities to order the Guangdong Customs to temporarily abolish the foreign rice import tax until the early rice harvest in June or July of next year, and then reinstate the tax in order to relieve the current panic over food. Yesterday, Yu Hanmou, Director of the Guangdong Pacification Office, and Huang Musong, Chairman of the Provincial Government, jointly sent a telegram to the central government, the original text of which is as follows: Director Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Guangdong Province's rice production has always been insufficient. Even in good years, it is only enough for a few months. This summer's floods have resulted in no hope of a harvest. The price of rice is rising every day, with each yuan only buying six or seven catties. At this time of rural bankruptcy, the lives of the people are difficult.

Guizhou Province Abolishes Exorbitant Taxes, Amounting to 1.28 Million Yuan Annually

Guiyang Correspondence: Since the Republic of China, there have been many changes and chaos, and the central government's policies cannot be unified. Various provinces have embraced military separatism and drained the pond to catch all the fish. Ordinary taxes are insufficient, and exorbitant taxes are flourishing. Guizhou, a corner of the country, is no exception. In recent years, the central government has been unified, Guizhou's provincial administration has been reformed, and the province has started anew with the people. The abolition of exorbitant taxes has been listed as the key to governance. The reporter believes that this kind of record should have accurate statistics, so he does not avoid the tediousness of detailing the names and figures of the exorbitant taxes that have been abolished in each county of this province, based on what can be investigated, as follows: At the end of the fourth year, a total of 160 types of donations and taxes were abolished, amounting to more than 100,000 yuan annually. In addition, those that were abolished uniformly throughout the province include the tobacco acreage tax in each county, amounting to 1.14 million yuan annually, and the national calendar tax in each county, which was too harsh and detailed to be statistically significant. As for this year, those newly ordered to be abolished include the provincial middle school deed tax surcharge collected on behalf of 94 counties including Chishui (because the provincial middle school is completely supported by the province), as well as the Chishui grain tax, the orphanage surcharge donation, the Wuchuan lacquer export donation, the Danjiang goods donation, the Qingxi market donation, and several types of Guiyang city stall donations. The statistics show that the total amount of exorbitant tax donations abolished before and after amounts to more than 1.28 million yuan annually. If we add the profits of the contractors and the embezzlement of the tax collectors, the number should be twice as much. At present, there are still many local donations and taxes in each county, but they are mostly used to fund local education or have other legitimate uses. If they were completely abolished suddenly, various local undertakings would inevitably be affected. The combing, sorting, and tracking of the orbit remains to be the effort of the financial authorities.

Wuxi A Villager Strangled to Death in a Dilapidated House

Gao A'xing, a 53-year-old villager from Shedu Dam Village, Di Rang Township, Zhang Zhenqiao, Luoshe, County, farmer, wife Wu, with four sons and one daughter. A'xing was weak and often bullied. On the 1st of this month, Wang Fuhai, a villager from Beitangli, Qianwang Township, and Wang Jinfu, a villager from Da'anqiao Township, Fushan Township, borrowed five yuan in legal currency from A'xing, but A'xing refused. The next day, Gao's wife, Wu, negotiated with the two and went to the Luoshe teahouse to reason, but to no avail. At this time, Gao A'xing suddenly disappeared and did not return until late at night. The day before yesterday, in the early morning, A'fu Niang, while passing by a broken three-room house in Shedu Dam Village, saw A'xing's body in the broken house. From the situation, he was strangled to death. A white belt was wrapped around his neck. Zhenjiang: Two Banks Rectify Subsidiary Currency

In view of the prevalence of private notes in the counties north of the Yangtze River in Jiangsu Province, and the deeply rooted malpractices they engendered, the Jiangsu Provincial Government had repeatedly issued strict prohibitions. However, there was a severe shortage of subsidiary currency in the market, and the need was extremely high. In order to eliminate private notes and facilitate the people, the Provincial Government, upon consulting the Ministry of Finance and obtaining its approval, authorized the Jiangsu Farmers Bank and the Jiangsu Bank to jointly issue subsidiary currency notes of 10-cent, 20-cent, and 50-cent denominations, totaling 3 million yuan, to provide relief. In accordance with the central government's approved method, they jointly provided cash and various guarantees as reserves, which were transferred to the Central Bank for storage and safekeeping. Since their issuance, they have circulated freely throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River. The Jiangsu Farmers Bank and Jiangsu Bank branches in various locations fully exchange them for legal currency, and public and private institutions alike universally accept them, providing convenience to merchants and the people. In the future, private notes will gradually be eliminated, which can be a great help in consolidating finance in Jiangsu Province. It is also reported that the 10-cent notes issued by the Xuzhou Ping City Official Money Bureau are also being fully exchanged by the two banks.

Elementary school students went out to solicit donations on one day, and patriotic citizens generously contributed. This round of donations is even more enthusiastic than before.

The Second Installment of Land Tax Begins Collection

Xiaoshan will begin collecting the second installment of the 25th year land tax on December 1, with a deadline of two months for full payment. Overdue payments will be subject to a late payment penalty of 2% of the total amount of the provincial and county regular and additional taxes due. If the payment is still not completed by the end of the year, a penalty of 3% will be added.

University Football Second Round: Guanghua vs. Jinan Today; 2:30 PM at Jinan University in Zhenru; Tongji vs. Fudan at Fudan

The Shanghai University Sports Federation football championship began on the 28th of last month. As for the Guanghua-Jinan match, although Jinan has the initial advantage of home field and its strength is also growing rapidly, Guanghua has been unusually strong this season, repeatedly achieving impressive results, and its future is unlimited. Western Youth Basketball: Qingguang Lost to McLing B Yesterday; 43 to 36

Two Western Education Basketball League games were played yesterday. The first game was between Mingqiang and Shakel in the regular division, which was played in four quarters. In the first quarter, Shakel attacked hard and won 14-7. In the second quarter, Mingqiang tried its best to resist and surprisingly showed impressive momentum, winning 11-5. In the third quarter, both sides were cautious and the score was very close. As a result, Shakel won again 8-6. In the last quarter, Mingqiang had a good performance, but Shakel scored continuously, so Mingqiang only took the lead by 10-9. The final result was a 34-34 tie, so overtime was played for three minutes. Shakel relied on Gu Lunsi's last shot to secure the victory, resulting in a 36-34 victory for Shakel. The other game was between Qingguang and McLing B in the independent division. In the first half, Qingguang took the lead and performed brilliantly, leading 11-8. Although McLing tried hard to catch up, Qingguang still won the first half 24-22. Switching sides, Qingguang was still very strong and led 28-24, and then led 30-27. However, due to a lack of stamina, McLing seized the opportunity to score 21-12, reversing the situation. The final result was 43-36, with McLing winning. Amateur Billiards League: Zhang Yingda Lost to Medina; Result 124 to 300

In the Shanghai Amateur Billiards League, Portugal and the International Recreation Club played a key match yesterday. Zhang Yingda, the main player of the International Club, and Medina of Portugal faced off at 6 PM. After one hour of competition, Medina defeated Zhang Yingda 300-124. Medina made 21 shots to reach the goal, averaging slightly less than 14 points per shot. The highest scores were 124, 53, 39, 21, 40, and 38. Zhang Yingda scored 23 and 24. In this 300-point short-distance goal, Medina scored over 20 points seven times, including 45 points and 39 points twice, which were achieved by unexpected luck. The Portuguese are very skilled in pocketing. Once they get into a rhythm, they continue to score. When they finally reached 300 points, the 56-point shot was not yet finished. Zhang Yingda is better at open shots than pocketing. He had bad luck yesterday, with many balls hitting the edge of the pocket. The goal was only 300 points, which gave the hero no room to maneuver. Zhang had no choice but to watch his defeat. As a result of the five-game match between the two teams, Portugal won.

Fudan University Held Yesterday; Chizhi Wins Over Wulong; Qixiu Wins Over Fudan; Jinan Wins Over Fudan

Qixiu Wins Over Fudan

The game between the Qixiu and Fudan women's basketball teams was the opening performance of last night, with Mr. Zhang Yousan, Dean of Studies of Fudan, making the opening throw. Fudan's defense was slightly lax, and Qixiu ended the first quarter with a score of 16-1, taking a huge advantage. In the second quarter, both sides defended tightly, and it was very difficult to score. Although Fudan launched a major counterattack, they only scored three goals, while Qixiu also scored two. Although Fudan pulled back two points, the distance was still large. In the third quarter, Fudan gradually made progress, still leading 5-2. In the last quarter, Qixiu won by a narrow margin of 4-2. Jinan Wins Over Fudan

The highlight of the evening was the game between Jinan and Fudan. The two sides were evenly matched, making it the most exciting page of the night. The referee was from Fudan. Fudan's Ma Zhou and Fu scored every time they shot, reversing the score to 15-12 at the end of the first half. Fudan's players tried their best to start scoring, but Cai Yanxiong scored again, leading by two points. Ma Zhou made one of one free throw, bringing the score to 21-20. Fudan chased to within one point again. Before long, Yin Guiren scored two consecutive shots, and Chen Zongqi also made two free throws. The score was still in the twenties. Jinan's Cai Wang was too hasty and lost two chances under the basket. After Wang Nanzhen made a free throw, Zhou Dayun chased to 24-26. Jinan urgently called a timeout, changed from attack to defense, and Kuang Yaoya seized the opportunity to score again, reversing the victory with a score of 28-24.

Chizhi Wins Over Wulong

The second act was the men's basketball performance between Chizhi and Wulong. Chen Changde and Wu Shijie were the referees. After the toss-up, Wulong's Wang Zhenlun scored first, and Wu Biqian scored two more, leading 6-0. After Chizhi called a timeout, Zhan Tingrui broke the deadlock. Before long, Chizhi's Chen Xuechong and Liang Yunming scored continuously, and instantly surpassed Wulong 10-6. But soon Wulong became active again, ending the first half with a score of 12-16, with Wulong in the lead. At the start of the second half, Chizhi suddenly rose up, surpassing Wulong 23-20. Wulong fought hard to cope, but Chizhi still took the lead. After 27-27, Chizhi became sharper again, and Wulong declined. After 37-34, Chizhi became more and more courageous, scoring four more goals in one breath, resulting in a 46-36 victory for Chizhi.

Thirteen-Mile Long Run: The Route Was Surveyed Yesterday; Starting Point: Intersection of White Lainan Road and Yi Dingpan Road; Held on New Year's Day Next Year

The first 13-mile long-distance race organized by the Marathon Promotion Association is scheduled to close registration on the 25th of this month and will be held on New Year's Day next year. The details of the association's preparations are recorded below:

Route

The race route was inspected yesterday and it was found that the originally planned route was about two miles longer, so it has now been changed to start at the intersection of White Lainan Road and Yi Dingpan Road, turn into Zhongshan Road, to Daxi Road, along Lincoln Road, Huo Bilan Road, pass through White Lainan Road, Beixinjing, Luo Biegen Road, Zhengjiaqiao, Hongqiao Road, Jiaotong University, turn north through Hague Road, turn into Yi Dingpan Road, and finally return to the front of the Qian Gong School on White Lainan Road as the finish line. The above-mentioned accurate route is now being drawn in detail and will be announced later.

Registration

The registration locations were originally set at Huade Soap Factory on Ouyang Road in the North District and Feisheng Radio Store at the Wujiaochang on Jisifei Road in the West District. Now, Referee Committee member Mr. Li Baojun, to facilitate the registration of players, has specially divided three more areas: the Central District is located next to the Xieqiao General Assembly Hall on Yanan Temple Road, Huadong Sports Equipment Company, the South Shanghai District is located at Yilin Bookstore, No. 1439 Zhonghua Road, Ximen, and the East Shanghai District is located at Hongxing Printing Bureau, No. 7-2 Dongxi Huade Road.

What Football and Basketball Players Should Read: New Books on Football and Basketball; Victory is Guaranteed After Reading

The football and basketball season has arrived, and players are working hard to practice. Instructors are also engaged in training players to exercise their bodies and win games. However, practice must be done with the latest methods in order to improve skills and win every game. The Diligence Bookstore at No. 277 Qipan Street and Wangping Street, Simalu, Shanghai, publishes the "Sports Series," which is popular throughout the country. Newly published football and basketball books include "Football Training Method," written by Wu Bangwei, head of the Zhenjiang Sports Field of Jiangsu Province, which details training methods, posture photos, and offensive diagrams, with more than 110 types, which is very suitable for beginners and instructors. Each book costs 90 cents. Mr. Wu also wrote "Football Rules Questions," which explains football rules in question-and-answer format. Each book costs 30 cents. There is also "The Art of Football Success" by the Englishman Hunt, which details various kicking methods of famous British football players. Each book costs 50 cents. "The Latest Football Rules" costs 8 cents per book. "The National Football Stars Record" costs 10 cents per book. Wu Bangwei also wrote "Basketball Training Method," which is clearly explained and has more than 100 photos, indicating basic basketball training methods. Each book costs 90 cents. Qian Yiqin, a sports instructor at the Lizhi Society, and Zhang Guoxun, a sports editor for the Mainland Newspaper, jointly translated "American Basketball New Techniques," which is the latest basketball play in the United States, using diagrams. Each book costs 75 cents. Song Junfu, director of sports at Shandong University, wrote "Women's Basketball Training Method," which is suitable for training female basketball players. Photos of female athletes are inserted to show the training methods. Each book costs 1.40 yuan. There are also "The Latest Men's Basketball Rules" and "The Latest Women's Basketball Rules," which are sold for 15 cents each. The above books are the only new football and basketball books in China. All instructors and players must read them. It is no exaggeration. The general distribution location of Diligence Bookstore is No. 392 Laoshenfu Road, Shanghai.
