Education News

Literacy and Remedial Textbooks in Various Provinces

When the Ministry of Education promulgated and implemented the Outline of Measures for Remedial Education for Out-of-School People in August of this year, it issued a circular to all provinces and cities, requiring them to universalize remedial education for out-of-school people within six years, starting from the 25th year, and to enforce compulsory enrollment. The textbooks for these people's schools are compiled and printed by the Ministry of Education and may be distributed free of charge, taking into account local conditions. The provinces and cities were also ordered to report the number of illiterate people and all plans to promote social education. As of now, except for Gansu, Henan, Ningxia, Xikang, Shanxi, Hebei, and Suiyuan, which only reported plans but not the number of illiterate people, Sichuan and Guangdong each had 500,000 illiterate people in the first semester of the 25th year. The Ministry of Education has issued 150,000 copies of the combined first and second volumes of textbooks for people's schools, totaling 500,000 copies. Shandong 360,000 (the number of illiterate people is the same as the number of textbooks, and the following will be abbreviated accordingly), Shaanxi 340,000, Jiangxi 240,000, Zhejiang, Hubei, and Fujian 150,000 each, Anhui 400,000, Hunan and Yunnan 100,000 each, Guizhou 50,000, Xinjiang 70,000, Qinghai 25,000, Chahar 20,000, Beijing and Tianjin 10,000 each, Qingdao 28,000, and Weihaiwei 2,000. The above 19 provinces and cities had a total of 3,205,000 illiterate people in the first semester of the 25th year. The Ministry of Education has issued a total of 3,205,000 copies of textbooks for people's schools. In addition, Guangxi has 1 million illiterate people this year and plans to completely eliminate illiteracy. The province has compiled textbooks for people's schools and the Ministry of Education has subsidized 10,000 yuan for printing expenses as an incentive. Jiangsu has 2,150,000 illiterate people in the first semester of this year (4.3 million for the whole year) and has compiled its own textbooks for people's schools. The Ministry of Education has subsidized 30,000 yuan. Nanjing has 25,000 illiterate people in this period and has compiled its own textbooks. The Ministry of Education has subsidized 1,000 yuan. The textbooks issued by the Ministry of Education will be used in the next semester. Shanghai has 170,000 illiterate people throughout the year (85,000 in this period) and has compiled its own textbooks. The Ministry of Education has subsidized 20,000 yuan. Cash subsidies for 14 provinces and cities, except for Nanjing, are all for the printing expenses of textbooks for one year. In total, the reported 23 provinces and cities had 5,975,000 illiterate people in the first semester of the 25th year, plus the unreported 7 provinces and cities, there are about 2 million, totaling about 7 million illiterate people. The whole year has about 14 million illiterate people, which has exceeded the 12 million that the Ministry of Education plans to eliminate.

Various Schools Donate to Aid Suiyuan

Daozhong Women's Middle and Elementary School: Daozhong Women's Middle and Elementary School held a one-day aid-Suiyuan movement starting in late October. Teachers donated 5% of their monthly salary, and students donated 10 or 20 cents each. Because the war cannot be ended in a short time, it is planned to raise funds for a long time and purchase other necessities. The collected 101 yuan, 24 cents was yesterday handed over to the administrative director Zhao Weiqin and the student representatives Zhou Shizhu and Zhang Yumei, etc., with a letter to this newspaper to be forwarded to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan Province for distribution to the front lines, to express their sincere condolences.

Zicai Elementary School: All the students of Zicai Elementary School on Bazilu in this city saved their daily candy money, totaling 17 yuan and 20 cents, and entrusted it to this newspaper to be remitted to General Fu Zuoyi at the front lines. Because the war in eastern and northern Suiyuan has started again recently, the school immediately held an expanded fundraising campaign to provide assistance.

Suzhou Library Prepares for Literature Exhibition

From January 1 to 7, the Suzhou Canglang Pavilion Provincial Library will hold an exhibition to showcase the cultural excellence of the Wu region, its beautiful scenery, and the achievements of its predecessors, which are worthy of emulation. However, in these rapidly changing times, there is a fear that this culture may decline. In order to elucidate and promote this culture and provide role models for young students, the organization and promotion of local literature is particularly urgent. Therefore, the Wu Chinese Literature Exhibition was initiated and approved by the Provincial Department of Education. It is scheduled to be held for seven days starting on January 1, 26th year. Letters are being sent to various libraries, collectors, and enthusiasts to solicit exhibits, and preparations are actively underway. It is reported that the scope of this solicitation includes the four counties of Wuxian, Wujiang, Kunshan, and Changshu, which are the former jurisdiction of Suzhou Prefecture. The categories of solicitation, the procedures for submitting exhibits, etc., are detailed in the exhibition regulations, which are recorded as follows: Purpose: To promote literature and advance scholarship. Venue: Suzhou Canglang Pavilion Main Library. Dates: January 1 to 7, 26th year. Scope of solicitation: Limited to items related to Wu Chinese (Wuxian, Wujiang, Kunshan, Changshu) literature. The categories are as follows: 1. Books, engravings, plates, manuscripts, annotations, transcriptions, local chronicles, genealogies, maps, portraits, historical sites, scenic spots. 2. Bronze and stone inscriptions, antiquities, original stones, rubbings, cultural artifacts, clothing. 3. Calligraphy and paintings, local sages, transients, monks, nuns. 4. Historical materials, revolution (such as portraits and relics of martyrs), politics (such as archives and registers), imperial examinations (such as genealogical records and application forms), academies (such as ink scrolls and examination papers). Submission Procedures: Applicants should fill out the exhibit registration form before December 15, 25th year, so that the exhibits can be cataloged. After the 16th, they should submit the exhibits to the library and obtain a receipt as proof. If there are many or valuable items, the library can send someone to pick them up. Applicants who wish to use a pseudonym or studio name instead of their own name should notify the library in advance. The library will comply accordingly. Exhibit Custody: The library is fully responsible for the custody of the exhibits during the exhibition period until they are returned. Return Procedures: Exhibits can be retrieved with the receipt within ten days after the exhibition. Valuable items can be returned by library personnel.

Local News

Cotton Yarn: Standard Yarn Reaches New High at Closing, Spot Transactions at 262.5 Yuan for Current Month, 1,200 Bales Transacted

The previously declining yarn market rebounded yesterday with a significant surge. The rationale for this surge is attributed to a shortage of spot goods. Only about a thousand bales remain in warehouses. Simultaneously, the Qingdao Japanese Cotton Mill, with 500,000 spindles, has completely ceased operations. Northern merchants are also procuring yarn, and merchants from Sichuan also have strong buying intentions. However, factories are struggling to supply enough spot goods, leading to heightened sentiment and rising market prices. December futures climbed above the 260 yuan mark, reaching a new high of 260.5 yuan.

Futures for all Months Increase by Six to Seven Yuan

At the opening of the standard yarn trading session, all months showed an upward trend. However, news of the landing of Japanese marines in Qingdao and the complete shutdown of the Qingdao yarn mill created uncertainty, as these two pieces of news seemed contradictory. After the second trading session, the December contract showed particularly strong upward momentum, approaching the 260 yuan mark. Many speculated that yarn prices in Qingdao were soaring, with merchants from Tianjin procuring spot yarn and those from Sichuan also making moves. As a result, the market became increasingly tight, advancing rapidly. Today, prices exceeded 260 yuan, with long-term contracts performing well at closing. Consequently, all months rose by 4.5 to 5.3 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. The market remained strong after the afternoon opening. Near-term contracts showed stronger upward momentum, while long-term contracts remained relatively stable. During the second afternoon session, rumors resurfaced, causing a sudden drop of 1.3 to 1.4 yuan. By the third closing, there were reports of 1,200 bales of spot yarn still being transacted, boosting morale. Prices for all days reached new highs. At closing, prices for all months rose by an additional 1.6 to 2.4 yuan compared to the morning closing. Selling orders included 2,000 bales from Juxing, 1,100 bales from Yuda, 2,400 bales from Zhenda, 950 bales from Minghua, 3,400 bales from Yicheng, 1,800 bales from Taichang, 1,850 bales from Yichang, 1,000 bales from Hengchang, 1,850 bales from Shengyuan, 1,700 bales from Changyu, 3,000 bales from Hengde, and 1,600 bales from Dachangcheng. Purchase orders included 1,750 bales from Hengyi, 3,700 bales from Dafeng, 3,550 bales from Mingde, 3,700 bales from Hexing, 8,750 bales from Changfeng, 1,050 bales from Tonghe, 1,300 bales from Jinchang, 2,000 bales from Shenji, 2,300 bales from Runkang, 2,000 bales from Fukang, and 2,000 bales from Xincheng. A comparison is provided below:

The sales of spot yarn are still considerable. It is estimated that all merchants bought a total of 1,210 bales throughout the day. The selling price increased by 2 yuan. Also Affected by the Qingdao Strike, Cotton Prices Feel Unsupported

The cotton market was originally flat. However, the yarn market has been rising daily, affecting the raw materials. However, the Qingdao yarn mill stoppage has negatively impacted sentiment, resulting in a stable market with moderated price increases. Factory demand is still sustainable.

Assisted by Period Yarn to Some Extent

At the opening of standard cotton trading, the market appeared sluggish and weak, as the complete shutdown of Qingdao yarn mills had a significant impact on sentiment. Additionally, the American and Indian cotton markets were trending downward. The number of buyers in the market was low. After the second session, the market rebounded slightly due to the positive performance of the yarn market. Consequently, prices for all months rose by 0.15 to 0.3 yuan compared to the previous day's closing. The market price was still uneven after the afternoon opening. Later, as yarn prices reached new highs, the market sentiment became volatile but firm. As a result, prices for all months rose by an additional 0.15 to 0.25 yuan compared to the morning closing. Selling orders included 2,800 dan from Shengyuan, 3,000 dan from Juxing, 10,700 dan from Mingde, 2,700 dan from Fengtai, 3,600 dan from Shenji, 3,600 dan from Yicheng, 3,000 dan from Yichang, 5,500 dan from Yongda, 7,900 dan from Yuanxingchang, 2,000 dan from Changji, and 2,000 dan from Changfeng. Purchase orders included 2,600 dan from Hexing, 4,600 dan from Yuda, 1,300 dan from Renfeng, 3,700 dan from Xiecheng, 6,500 dan from Xincheng, 6,000 dan from Changhe, 5,000 dan from Zhenda, 2,700 dan from Gengfeng, 2,900 dan from Dachangcheng, and 2,400 dan from Tonghe. A comparison is provided below:

Arrivals Consist Mainly of General Grade Cotton

Spot cotton consumption is slightly sluggish, and factory demand has turned sluggish. The source of cotton is 300 bales of Yaohua cotton.

American Cotton Ends the Day Firm

American cotton prices opened down 7 to 12 points for all months, with trading being relatively slow. Liverpool's consumption was poor, and the political situation in England was unstable. The December contract had 14 delivery notices, prompting bulls to close out positions and foreign merchants to short sell, all contributing to the early morning price decline. Later, industry players bought in, short positions covered, and the stock market was strong, leading to a market rebound. New accounts from outside the industry gradually increased, but buyers remained cautious. The closing was firm, with spot prices rising by 1 point and futures falling by 3 points to rising by 2 points. English cotton fell by 1 point in spot and 5-6 points in futures. Indian cotton speculators bought in, driven by short selling. Later, prices weakened due to poor consumption in Liverpool. Bengal and Oomra fell by 1 rupee, while White Broach fell by 0.75 rupees. Original telegram recorded (from the 3rd).

According to a telegram from Bombay, the opening forecast for the 4th was White Broach at 219 rupees, Oomra at 198 rupees, and Bengal at 160.25 rupees, all unchanged.

Osaka telegram, 4th: Three-grade futures yarn rose by 0.7 to fall by 1.1 yuan, with near-term at 244.7 yuan and long-term at 217.9 yuan. Cotton futures fell by 0.25 to 0.55 yuan, with near-term at 67.1 yuan and long-term at 67.9 yuan.

Piece Goods: Cotton Cloth is Easy to Rise, Difficult to Fall, Bleached Cloth Rises Nearly One Yuan, Yesterday Prices of Various Goods Rose Several Jiao

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market was characterized by strong sales in both the north and south. Labor unrest broke out again at the Japanese-owned Nisshin Cotton Mill, and yarn prices, which had softened slightly the day before, rebounded sharply yesterday. Sentiment was unanimously firm, with strong buying intentions, leading to purchases as prices rose, causing the market to soar. Coarse cloth, which had previously seen sluggish sales in the north, experienced a relatively moderate increase in prices for heavyweight varieties. However, with current inventories depleted, the price increase has become rapid. Yesterday, the market rose sharply by 0.3 to 0.4 yuan (per bolt). Lightweight fine cloth rose by 0.2 yuan, while plain fine cloth and dyed cloth rose by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan (per bolt). Flannel and Zhigong velvet also continued to rise by 2.5 li (per yard). Bleached cloth, currently out of season, had a rather low market price. However, the rising prices of new gray cloth from factories were very rapid, creating a significant gap. As the peak sales season for long-distance customers is approaching, high-end bleached cloth inventories have rapidly increased by nearly 1 yuan (per bolt). Printed Zhigong, Serge, Colored Zhigong, and Satin, although off-season, have significantly higher gray cloth prices than before. Sentiment is optimistic, and sales have also slightly improved, with market prices rebounding by 0.2, 0.3, and 0.5 yuan per bolt, respectively. Japanese firms such as Toyo Menka Kaisha, Nisshin, and Ito have collectively issued nearly 2,000 pieces of white fine cloth and fine twill for February and March, with prices also increasing gradually. However, they are still about 0.5 yuan lower than the current spot market prices. The January quota has already been exhausted, and factories are shipping out spot goods daily, but they are still insufficient to meet customer demand.

Woolen Fabric Orders See Resurgence, Market Goods are Scarce and Insufficient for Sales, Shipments are Particularly Heavy in March and April

Yesterday, the woolen fabric market remained excellent. Local and inland merchants continued to show strong interest in purchasing men's and women's colored overcoat woolen fabrics, with particularly strong sales. Western firms had robust shipments, and domestic products were largely insufficient to meet sales demand. Benchmark prices were firm both openly and secretly. Merchants were able to profit from most of the goods they had previously acquired. Recognizing the scarcity of market goods and active sales, merchants placed more orders with Western firms, leading to a resurgence in ordering activity. Merchants were actively ordering goods for spring, summer, autumn, and winter, especially English and Japanese goods for shipment in March and April of next year.

Food: Flour Prices All Hit Four Yuan, Outside Buyers' Enthusiastic Purchases Cause Unusual Surge

Yesterday, the flour market, after opening in the morning, displayed an initial period of stability, followed by a sharp surge across all months. Foreign wheat quotations from Chicago and Canada were down 0.1 to 0.2 jiao, while Liverpool also experienced a significant drop of 0.1 to 0.2 pence. Therefore, when prices opened, the current month showed weakness, opening at only 0.96 yuan, down a fen from the previous day. However, starting with the January contract, outside buyers drove eager purchases, causing prices to jump by 0.2 to 0.3 fen immediately. After the second session, factories covered their near-term positions, pushing prices above the 4 yuan mark. Factories were shorting long-term contracts, so while buying interest was strong, the increase was more moderate. When the market opened in the afternoon, the current month saw inquiries from merchant houses, and factories also slightly covered, raising prices as high as 4.04 yuan. However, bulls closed out positions, causing prices to fall back by 0.1 to 0.2 fen. Large outside players continued to buy eagerly in the long-term contracts, and market sentiment continued to rise. Given the current situation, domestic supplies are scarce and foreign wheat prices are not favorable, so market sentiment is unlikely to stabilize.

Wheat Market Stable

Yesterday, the wheat market, after opening in the morning, showed an initial period of stability, followed by a firm trend across all months. Foreign wheat quotations unanimously reported declines. However, market sentiment was firm due to domestic wheat prices not easing and the purchasing and stockpiling by the military and civilians in the northern regions being stronger than in this port. Therefore, despite the fall in foreign wheat, market sentiment remained firm, with only minor fluctuations of 0.1 to 0.2 fen across all months. When the market opened in the afternoon, sentiment improved again. There were reports of slight futures purchases by Tianjin factories, and merchants from Shaanxi continued to purchase spot wheat, leading to increased transactions and a market rebound of 0.3 to 0.4 fen. However, the market value was already high, and buyers were inevitably watching, so the upward trend gradually leveled off, which was not without reason. In the spot wheat market, there were no official transactions due to customers selling and factories not being interested. It was reported that merchants from Shaanxi purchased more than 20 tons, with Gaoyou wheat opening at 6.55 yuan and Yanghe wheat at 6.6 yuan.

Customer White Rice Sales Rebound Yesterday in Guangdong

Yesterday's customer white rice market situation: the supply continued unabated, and most of the owners intended to sell. Therefore, although there were actions such as strikes and transport blockades for river rice, the market price of customer white rice did not improve. Because the main route of customer white rice is the Guangdong sales market, and Guangdong has not had a smooth channel for a long time, the market showed that supply exceeded demand, and the situation immediately trended downward. But the arrival volume yesterday and the day before was slightly reduced, and the digestion was still active, so the market can still stand. Shantou and this street's digestion are all active. In the afternoon, Henan continued to handle it, and the market situation began to show signs of being popular. The opening throughout the day was 2,673 bags of Gan rice, 1,050 bags of Xiang rice, 1,720 bags of Wenhe Yong various rice, and 500 bags of factory yuan. The price was similar to the previous market.

Japonica Rice Store Sales are Watching

(Yesterday, the source of various gangs in Shanghai South was slightly sparser than before. A total of more than 80 households arrived, with more than 16,000 names in total. Among them, more than 50 households were Bo Dao, but the sales market on this street also suddenly declined slightly. Pingjin Qiyan and other gangs only handled more than 6,000 bags of Bo Dao (and more than 1,000 bags of thick japonica, so the market turned flat again. As a result, the market conditions of thick and thin japonica did not show any glory or shame. Due to the lack of goods, Dujian continued to perform well for 5 cents. Yang Jian was flat, Yinyuan was high and low,

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, the chairman of the rice industry consulted with his colleagues that more than 200 rice boats that are currently being detained in Jiading County. The Municipal Social Bureau forwarded a telegram to the Provincial Government, hoping that they would be released within two or three days, so the public's hearts were stable. Although the stores did not have much inventory, they heard this news and that a large number of rice boats would come to Shanghai, so they instead stood by and watched and did not buy. The various goods were sluggish and did not digest. The market conditions of high-quality japonica were stable due to the lack of goods, and the price of high-quality japonica was small. The price of Yang Jian was nearly a tenth lower, and the price of Bu Dujian was a few cents lower. Securities: Government Bond Market Fluctuates Greatly

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange government bond market continued to be weak, and the trend continued to brew. The public's minds were even more confused by the current situation. However, the bulls and bears were fiercely opposed to each other, and there were large amounts of trading in and out. As a result, the market price fluctuated more violently, and the amount of chips thrown out on the table was very strong, and the market price fell across the board. However, because the bulls and bears were both strong, the rise and fall in the short term was still within a certain range. Yesterday morning, the market opened very weakly. Grade E was heavily sold off in No. 3, and it fell sharply by 5 to 6 cents, and retail investors also sold off in groups. Grades D and B also fell by 5 cents to 4 cents. In the second session, the trend turned firmer, and Nos. 10, 22, 47, etc. bought in strongly, while Nos. 5, 10, 5, etc. sold off. The market price rebounded across the board from Grade E by 1 to 4.5 cents. In the afternoon, the market price went from firm to weak. Grade D No. 35 had a very strong appetite and rose by 5 cents to 4 cents. Long-term contracts in Grade C rose, and retail investors sold off. Nos. 35 and 10 also turned to selling. Grades A and B fell again by about 1 cent. At the close, Nos. 45 and 18 suddenly had a large amount of selling, and the market price continued to decline weakly, all down by a little over a tenth to 6 cents. However, Nos. 10 and 32 bought in quite a bit. The result for the whole day was a uniform decline of 1.5 to 4 cents. Grade A for this month rose by 5 cents. City Government Mobilizes Over 60,000 Strong Laborers to Conduct Citizen Labor Services, Mainly for River Dredging and Levee Construction, Regular and Separate Extensive Publicity Campaigns

The Da Gong She reports: This city, upon order, is conducting the 25th year winter citizen labor service, which the city government has ordered the Engineering, Social Affairs, and Public Safety Bureaus to jointly formulate measures for, establishing the Shanghai Citizen Labor Service Committee. An office has been set up at the Aviation Association in the central district of the city, with Mayor Wu as the chairman. Currently, all preparatory work has been completed, and within days, over 60,000 strong laborers from designated areas will be mobilized to dredge rivers and construct levees. The details are recorded as follows:

City Government Proclamation

Shanghai Municipal Government Proclamation No. 387. According to the report from the City Labor Service Committee: This committee has completed the planning for the 25th year winter labor service project, which has been approved by the first meeting. The project is divided into ten districts: Wusong, Yinhang, Jiangwan, Yinxiang, Zhenru, Pusong, Gaoqiao, Gaoxing, Lihang, and Caojing. The main goal is to dredge the main rivers in each district and construct embankments to provide practical benefits for water conservancy, transportation, and sanitation. The labor service period is from December 1st of this year to March 31st of the 26th year. All males in the respective areas between the ages of 18 and 40 must participate in the service. Those residing within the dredging area must serve for a maximum of five days, while those assisting outside the dredging area must serve for a maximum of three days. Participants must provide their own meals and digging tools, as clearly stipulated in the implementing rules. As the start date is approaching, the engineering plan has been compiled and submitted for review, requesting prompt notification for public convenience. A copy of the 25th year winter labor service project plan is attached. Therefore, in addition to the order, the 25th year winter labor service project plan is listed below for the information of all citizens. This proclamation, December 2nd, 25th year of the Republic of China, Mayor Wu Tiecheng.

Engineering Plan

The 25th year winter labor service project plan includes: (1) Wusong District: Dredge Zhangjianbang and Shengjiabang; (2) Yinhang District: Dredge Yuanchang River and Echanpu, construct Qianjiabang embankment; (3) Jiangwan District: Dredge Xietang; (4) Yinxiang District: Dredge the western section of Yangshupu Qiujiang; (5) Zhenru District: Dredge Mudu Port, Qiujiang, and Taopu; (6) Pusong District: Dredge the southern section of the Shahe River and Shuangyang Port; (7) Caojing District: Dredge Shangtongtang; (8) Gaoqiao District: Dredge the southern section of Huangao Port, Qingpu Port, and Xingang, construct Dongtang and Shitang; (9) Gaoxing District: Dredge Hutangbang, Xiantangbang Chunshupu, and Hengbang; (10) Lihang District: Dredge Zhujia Ditch, construct the embankment of Majiabang in the 44th map.

Service Laborers

The number of laborers serving in each district this year, according to the Public Security Bureau's investigation, is approximately as follows: Wusong 3,463, Yinhang 4,855, Zhenru 6,757, Gaoqiao 6,287, Gaoxing 2,825, Jiangwan 6,258, Lihang 2,400, Caojing 7,577, Yinxiang 7,597, Pusong 12,374, totaling 60,393.

Labor Committee

The members of the Shanghai Labor Service Committee include Chairman Wu Tiecheng, members Yu Hongjun, Zhou Yongneng, Shen Yi, Xu Fu, Cai Jinjun, Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Ji Zhangjian, Huang Renzhi, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, General Manager Hong Qi, Deputy General Managers Xu Guansan, Wu Huanru, secretaries Dai Erjing, Zou Zhigao, Yu Zhenhui, Li Zemin, Xu Shaoxiu, Xu Zuming, Li Shigen, and the heads of each district: Wusong District Head Tang Chengzong, Deputy Head Shang Shouye, Yinhang District Zhu Jiajun, Hu Wencai, Jiangwan District Gu Shanzhang, Liu Xirong, Yinxiang District Li Zhuoren, Chen Zhendong, Zhenru District Hong Lanxiang, Wen Chunpu, Pusong District Dong Pingxing, Cheng Zhongjin, Caojing District Yang Xinzheng, Yang Jingxiang, Gaoqiao District Tang Jinghuan, Jia Zhensheng, Gaoxing District Pan Hongding, Wen Zilin, Lihang District Zhang Qiwen, Wen Zilin.

Regular Publicity

The Shanghai Labor Service Committee, to ensure that citizens deeply understand the importance of labor service and are happy to serve, has specifically scheduled dates for each district head to invite principals of schools in their respective districts, responsible personnel of agricultural associations, map directors, local bailiffs, and enthusiastic local individuals to hold discussion meetings to discuss publicity matters. Shanghai-Guangdong Wireless Telephone to Open for Calls This Morning; Mayors Wu and Zeng to Conduct Telephone Courtesy at 9:00 AM; Shanghai, Wuhan, and Guangdong to Open for Interconnected Calls at 10:00 AM

The Shanghai-Guangdong long-distance wireless telephone service, sponsored by the Ministry of Communications, has been actively prepared by both Shanghai and Guangdong and has been completed. The two sides have conducted continuous trial calls, and the sound is quite clear. It is now scheduled to begin operation this morning. There will be no ceremony; only at 7:00 AM, the International Wireless Radio Station of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications will first conduct a trial call with the Guangdong Long-Distance Radio Station. At 9:00 AM, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng will separately conduct telephone courtesy with Huang Musong, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government, and Zeng Yangfu, Mayor of Guangzhou, and exchange congratulatory messages. At 10:00 AM, it will be officially opened for business, providing telephone service for the public. At the same time, Shanghai, Guangdong, and Wuhan will begin interconnected calls today, which will be more convenient for people from all walks of life. It is truly a new contribution to China's transportation. The main points of the telephone service are recorded as follows: (1) Types of calls: divided into registered, person-to-person, and collect calls, all with regular and expedited options. Expedited calls will always be connected first. (2) Call time is in three-minute units; less than three minutes is charged as three minutes, and more than three minutes but less than six minutes is charged as six minutes. (3) Call charges: Shanghai, Guangdong, and Wuhan have different prices, with a maximum of 13.2 yuan in national currency per three minutes and a minimum of six yuan and 5.1 yuan.

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued a notice yesterday, stating: "In response to the Ministry of Communications' concerns, the Shanghai-Guangdong wireless telephone service will be opened for calls on December 5th, and the business hours will be tentatively set from 7:00 AM to 11:00 PM daily. Please comply accordingly." Therefore, the business will be officially opened from this month. The three-minute call price for calls between Guangzhou and Shanghai is 5.5 yuan in national currency, and the price for calls within the Shanghai Special Zone is 6 yuan in national currency. This is hereby announced.

Thoughts on the Memorial of the Zhaohe Uprising

— Yang Hu

Twenty-one years have passed since the Zhaohe Uprising. Recalling the past and looking to the future, I cannot help but feel deeply moved again. Therefore, I express my thoughts and tell my fellow countrymen: The Xinhai Revolution, which overthrew the Manchu Qing, was only a preliminary goal. After overthrowing the Manchu Qing, we must always guide the national power back to the people, abolish unequal treaties externally, and strive for both material and psychological construction internally, so that the country can enter a truly free and equal realm. Therefore, on the day the Republic of China was established, the Premier of our party showed this revolutionary proposition to the future. Unfortunately, the party members of that day were weak in will, fearful of difficulties, and content with the status quo, deceived by the rhetoric of "the revolutionary army rises, the revolutionary party disappears," and no longer adhered to the initial revolutionary beliefs. As a result, the revolutionary cause suffered a great setback in both substance and spirit. From the second year of the Republic of China, Yuan Shikai carried out large loans, recruited troops and purchased weapons, cultivated party members, and eliminated dissidents. When his wings were completed, he did not hesitate to overthrow the Republic of China and declare himself emperor. In order to seek foreign aid, he did not hesitate to sign traitorous treaties, opening up opportunities for powerful neighbors to covet, and almost causing the disaster of national subjugation and extinction. Today, the national crisis is so serious. How can we know that it was not Yuan Shikai's momentary mistake that accumulated and formed? If the party members of that day could all understand the revolutionary proposition, obey the leader's orders, and not fear difficulties or be content with the status quo, Yuan Shikai, although he thought of stealing the divine weapon and satisfying his dictatorial desires, would not be able to act recklessly and do whatever he wanted. Therefore, the Zhaohe Uprising's opposition to Yuan Shikai was also to alert those who did not revolutionize or pretended to revolutionize to their ignorance and harm to the country. This is one. For thousands of years, Chinese scholars and officials have been deceived by the benefits of the art of diplomacy, so they have become skilled in seizing, coercing, and tempting, which has become the worldly skill of Chinese scholars and officials. When Yuan Shikai was in power, he gathered all of this into one. What he sought in politics was not to benefit the country and the people, but to cultivate party members for personal gain. What he associated with in society was not righteousness and sympathy, but conflicts of interest. Therefore, ambitious people used treacherous strategies as a ladder to seek advancement, and scholars all over the world ran around for fame and gain. Therefore, when Yuan Shikai proclaimed himself emperor, countless shameless people submitted memorials urging him to advance, and even beggars organized groups to write letters on the issue of changing the national system. The ridiculousness and absurdity were unmatched. Yuan Shikai was complacent, thinking that all the heroes in the world were in his shell, but he did not know that there were still many patriots in our party who raised their arms and shouted at the Huangpu River. Therefore, the Zhaohe Uprising's opposition to Yuan Shikai was also to destroy the decadent psychology of the scholars and officials of that time, not only to bomb away Yuan Shikai's body, but also to bomb away the ideas of power and tricks on which Yuan Shikai's spirit relied. This is two. From the situation at the time of the uprising, the soldiers who participated in the uprising, including myself, were only more than thirty, while the enemy's military strength was strong and the land and sea defenses were strict. The disparity between the few and the many, and the different strengths, meant that the failure was determined on the day of the uprising. However, the soldiers of the uprising strengthened their will, expanded their perseverance, and shouted loudly, hoping to die. This was because they were inspired by the Premier's decree that if they did not succeed, they would die for righteousness. This determination to die for righteousness was the most valuable treasure for saving the country and the people, and it could guide and develop the revolutionary forces latent in various inland areas, until Yunnan rose up and Yuan Shikai was overthrown. Therefore, the Zhaohe Uprising's opposition to Yuan Shikai was also to enlighten that the success of the revolution and the future of the Chinese nation standing independently in the world must all be due to the determination to die for righteousness. This is three. In summary, the Zhaohe Uprising had a significant impact on the party, the country, and the nation. Today, the national crisis is deepening, but fortunately we have Chiang Kai-shek, who still upholds the consistent spirit of leading the Zhaohe Uprising and makes unremitting efforts to save the country. May our countrymen never forget the historical lessons of the Zhaohe Uprising, tread on the blood of the martyrs, and advance at full speed under the leadership of Chiang Kai-shek to promote our nation and save our country. Then the soldiers of the Zhaohe Uprising, whether alive or dead, will feel gratified.

He is currently the president of the International Historical Society and recently lectured at Harvard University and Stanford University in the United States.

Zhang Fang Visited Various Circles Last Night to Report on the Henan Disaster and Request Relief

Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Relief Commission, and Chang Zizhen, a standing committee member, have come to Shanghai due to the severity of the disaster in Henan Province and the urgent need for relief. They specifically visited charitable organizations in the city to seek assistance. Last night, a special reception was held at the Hua'an Building for prominent figures from all walks of life in Shanghai. During the gathering, Mr. Zhang Fang reported on the disaster situation and relief measures. The details are recorded below:

Invited Guests

The invitees included Mayor Wu (represented by Li Dachao), Yang Xiaotian, Wang Yiting, Chu Huiseng, Wen Lanting, Gu Xinyi, Jiang Yiping, Lin Kanghou, Wang Boqi, Yu Qiaqing, Ye Gongchuo, Xue Dubi, Zhao Jinqing, Chen Guangfu (represented by Zhu Ruqian), Qu Wenliu, Huang Hanzhi, Song Hanzhang (represented by Ou Yongkang), Lu Liankui, Zhang Weiruo, Zhang Xiaolin, Xu Xinliu (represented by Zhang Yucheng), and more than seventy others.

Mr. Zhang's Address

During the gathering, Zhang Fang reported, saying, "Due to geographical reasons, Henan Province has been suffering from either floods or droughts almost every year. We are not unfamiliar with the assistance from all sectors of Shanghai. On behalf of the people of Henan, I would like to express my deep gratitude. This year, Henan Province has suffered another drought, which is particularly severe in western Henan, affecting more than nine million people. The harvest of farmland is less than 10%. Although the province has actively handled the disaster relief, due to our weak strength, we have to rely on the rescue from enthusiastic people in the country. Henan Province occupies a very important position in the country. The disaster has not only caused extreme suffering to the people but also has a great impact on public security. Therefore, the province has formulated a concrete plan for disaster relief and hopes to implement it step by step with the assistance of all sectors in Shanghai."

Guests' Response

Mayor Li Dachao then delivered a speech of thanks on behalf of Mayor Wu, saying, "Henan occupies a very important position in history and geography. All sectors of Shanghai are very concerned about the severe disaster situation. We hope that the newly organized charitable organizations in the city will have concrete relief methods for the severe disaster in Henan and send personnel to express condolences. The government authorities also hope to allocate huge sums of money to fundamentally relieve the disaster in Henan. Finally, on behalf of everyone, I would like to thank the host for this grand banquet."

Severe Disaster Situation

According to another report, Henan Province has not rained for several months since this autumn. The autumn harvest has not yielded any grain, and spring wheat has not been sown. In the most severely affected areas of the province, about forty counties are in a state of destitution, which is extremely tragic. Mr. Zhang Fang has asked for leave from his post in Jiangxi to come to Shanghai to describe the disaster situation to various charitable organizations, seeking donations. He also carries a draft of a plan to be presented to the Executive Yuan for work-relief, which is comprehensive and thoughtful, and speaks to both immediate and long-term concerns. Its main points are (1) The fundamental solution to drought is to develop water conservancy; (2) Developing water conservancy can reduce droughts and floods; (3) Work-relief can ensure that funds are not wasted. In thousands of words, it is not only a plan for disaster relief in Henan Province but also a good strategy for local public security. After consultations in Shanghai, Mr. Zhang will go to Luoyang to meet with Chairman Chiang to personally report on the defense situation and disaster relief measures in Henan.

Preparations for the Capital Express Are Complete and Can Be Implemented on Schedule

The Jing-Hu and Hu-Hang-Yong Railway Bureau, in accordance with the instructions of the Ministry of Railways, will operate the "Capital Express" between Nanjing and Shanghai. All preparations are generally complete and will be officially implemented on schedule after several more solemn tests. The preparations and test run are recorded as follows:

Historical Speed

Because the Beijing-Shanghai Railway's traffic equipment follows the old system, many signals and switches are not complete, so the traffic speed is extremely limited. The prescribed maximum speed between stations is 80 kilometers per hour. The prescribed maximum speed when passing facing switch points is 48 kilometers per hour. In addition, the entire line, except for the Shanghai to Nanxiang section, which has been double-tracked, is single-tracked. In addition, there are many stations, long stopping times, and many train times and meeting times, so it is not easy to shorten the travel time. In addition, there are level crossings with various highways along the line, and speeding is very likely to cause danger. However, since 1931, the travel time of each train on the Beijing-Shanghai line has been shortened again and again. Taking the special express train as an example, the revised timetable on March 1, 1933, was 7 hours and 48 minutes, the revised timetable in June was 6 hours and 50 minutes, the revised timetable on September 1 was 6 hours and 20 minutes, and the revised timetable on December 21, 1935, was 5 hours and 50 minutes. In May of this year, the Minister instructed that the research on shortening the travel time of the special express train between Beijing and Shanghai be continued, hoping to reduce the entire journey to four hours.

Three Test Runs

The bureau followed the ministry's instructions and first ordered Chief Wang of the Locomotive Department to use a Class C locomotive to haul six passenger cars for a test run on June 9th and 10th, stopping briefly at the four stations of Wuxian, Wuxi, Wujin, and Zhenjiang. The result was that the actual time required for the up train (from Shanghai to Beijing) was 251 minutes, and the actual time required for the down train (from Beijing to Shanghai) was 256 minutes. Later, Chief Wang of the Locomotive Department, Chief Huai Dehao of the Works Department, and Chief Xiao of the Traffic Department were ordered to conduct a joint test run on the 18th and 19th, using a Class C locomotive to haul six passenger cars, as before. The result was that the actual time required for the up train was 252 minutes, and the actual time required for the down train was 255 minutes. Summarizing the two test runs, the maximum speed between stations was approximately 80 kilometers per hour, and the speed when passing facing switch points was between 55 kilometers and 60 kilometers per hour. The stopping time at the four stations took approximately 18 minutes in total. However, it was summer at the time, so this was possible. If it were winter, it would be more difficult to burn the steam, and it would be necessary to provide warm steam to the passenger cars, and the restrictions of normal engineering would be unavoidable. Therefore, the actual travel time for the entire journey between Beijing and Shanghai would be more than this. On September 15, Chief Gan of the Locomotive Department and Chief Huai Dehao of the Works Department, together with the relevant personnel from the Beijing-Xixi-Shanghai sections, accompanied Dr. Lull and Von Rochow, German consultants of the Ministry of Railways, to conduct the third test run with a Class C locomotive hauling six passenger cars. The actual time required from Beijing to Shanghai was 259 minutes.

Improvement of Equipment

The results of the test run showed that it was still possible to shorten the travel time between Beijing and Shanghai. However, in order to actually operate passenger trains, it was necessary to first improve the traffic equipment. According to the estimate of the Works Department, if the standard of 4 hours for the entire journey is to be met immediately, the entire line must be uniformly relaid with heavy steel rails and new sleepers, and the bridges must be reinforced and new signals must be replaced. The total cost is approximately 4.29 million yuan in national currency. If the standard of 4 hours and 50 minutes is temporarily used, the required funds are approximately 750,000 yuan in national currency. It will still be handled in two parts. First, approximately 190,000 yuan in national currency is needed, which was approved by the Ministry of Railways on August 18. First, a trial run will be conducted according to the standard of 4 hours and 50 minutes. Therefore, all the improvement projects of traffic equipment will be started. The important ones are (1) Installation of warning signals, a total of 37 stations. (2) Installation of switch locks, all contracted by Xi Fuji. (3) Adding sleepers, the original 14 sleepers were padded for each steel rail, and now 2 are added to each, for a total of 56,700. (4) Paving the road, using 15,250 cubic meters of road bedding. In addition, the roadbed ditches were also improved and sorted out, using 9,000 cubic meters of sandstone and 2,875 cubic meters of sheet stone. As for the awarding of road signs at each station, it has been changed to an automatic method. In addition, one train of locomotives required is being reinforced and renovated. Class C locomotives are used, but the wheel diameter of the leading wheel of this type of locomotive is only 107 mm. After the speed is increased, there is a real fear that it will be easier to heat up, and it is planned to replace it with a roller bearing axle box. The vehicles include first-class passenger cars (with two dining cars, two second-class passenger cars, two third-class passenger cars, and one long car for heating, luggage, and mail). Each passenger car has been equipped with a heating oil tank to avoid burning the axles. Thirty-three new passenger car chassis have been purchased, and one train of the future "Capital Express" will use all the latest equipment passenger cars. In addition, the International Sleeping Car Company plans to add the latest European and American first-class parlor cars to the "Capital Express," which is under negotiation.

Prescribed Timetable

The "Capital Express" timetable has been submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval as follows: (1) The down train is train No. 1, departing from Nanjing Xiaguan Station at 17:30 every day, passing through Zhenjiang West Station, Wujin Station, Wuxi Station, and Wuxian Station, and arriving at Shanghai North Station at 22:20, the whole journey takes 4 hours and 50 minutes. (2) The up train is train No. 2, departing from Shanghai North Station at 8:00 every day, stopping at Wuxian Station, Wuxi Station, Wujin Station, and Zhenjiang West Station, and arriving at Nanjing Xiaguan Station at 12:48, the whole journey takes 4 hours and 48 minutes. That is, the "Capital Express" train will run from Shanghai to Nanjing every morning and return from Nanjing to Shanghai every afternoon.

Ticketing Method

The "Capital Express" will still charge special express ticket prices, and the principle is to ensure that each passenger has a seat. Therefore, the ticketing method has been separately determined and submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval. (1) Tickets for all classes of passenger cars on the "Capital Express" will be sold by the ticket office according to the number of seats. The detailed method is as follows: (A) The departure station of each train should reserve seats according to the number specified in the following table, to prepare for selling tickets to each stop along the way. (1) The up train North Shanghai Station reserves seats for each station: 4 first class, 8 second class, and 16 third class for Wuxian; 2 first class, 4 second class, and 8 third class each for Wuxi, Wujin, and Zhenjiang West. (2) The down train Nanjing Station reserves seats for each station: 4 first class, 8 second class, and 16 third class for Zhenjiang West; 2 first class, 4 second class, and 8 third class each for Wujin, Wuxi, and Wuxian. (B) Each stop along the way can sell tickets at any time according to the above regulations, but if the number of seats is sold out, it must wait for the train to depart from the previous station and notify the remaining vacant seats by telephone before selling tickets again. (C) The above reserved seats can still be sold when they do not hinder passengers boarding midway. (D) After each train departs, the departure station should notify the first stop by telephone of the details of the vacant seats of each class (the passengers arriving at the first stop and the seats reserved by the reservation are included in the vacant seats), so that the station can sell tickets according to the number (this number must not be less than the number reserved in item (A)). At the same time, the departure station will telegraph each station concerned with the details of the tickets of each class sold to each station. When the train departs from the first stop, the second stop will notify each station concerned with the details. In this way, each station can determine the number of tickets that can be sold. (2) Those who hold round-trip tickets, domestic tour tickets, or tickets purchased in advance, if taking the "Capital Express" train, must contact the ticket office to arrange seats. The date of the vehicle will be stamped by the ticket office and included in the number of tickets sold. (3) Once all the prescribed tickets have been sold out, each station should immediately stop selling tickets and hang a "Sold Out" sign. (4) Each travel agency is granted a certain number of seats for each class of vehicle according to the sleeper car method (but limited to the two departure stations). After inquiring about passengers taking the "Capital Express" train, it must be noted that the train number is stamped when selling tickets. The agency should notify the ticket office by telephone of the seat situation 10 minutes before departure so that statistics can be compiled. As for the three cases of traveling without a ticket, traveling beyond the station, and traveling beyond the class, tickets are still allowed to be supplemented in accordance with the regulations. However, the seat should first be given to passengers who purchased tickets at the station, so when there are no seats, they should still give way. The Ministry of Railways has been approved for record.

The Ministry of Finance Approves the Shanghai Joint Association's Decision to Stop Industrial and Commercial Loans

The First Special District Citizens' Joint Association received a reply from the Ministry of Finance, Qian Zi No. 11516, which stated: "The submission on November 17, 1936, requesting approval to postpone the closing of the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee for adjustment purposes, has been received. The Ministry established the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee last year for the purpose of rescuing Shanghai's industrial and commercial sectors. For a year, Shanghai's small industrial and commercial sectors have been revitalized through the Committee's loan rescue. Recently, the Committee has repeatedly stated that small industrial and commercial sectors in Shanghai in need of loans have mostly borrowed, those applying for loans recently mostly lack both assets and credit, and the market is gradually improving. Continuing would not be relevant to the market, and the Committee requests approval to close its operations, etc. The Ministry has verified that the situation is factual, and hereby orders the cessation of loans. This request should not be discussed further. This approval is dated December 3, 1936, and is signed by Minister Kong Xiangxi."

Hui Muslim Representatives came to Shanghai regarding the Nanjing University Land Dispute

Reported to the congregation yesterday

Nanjing Central University has selected more than 2,000 mu of mountainous land outside the Zhonghua Gate of Nanjing to build a new campus, including thousands of Hui Muslim graves, which are scheduled to be confiscated, which has aroused serious negotiations among Hui Muslims from all over the country. There are many Hui Muslims from Nanjing living in Shanghai, who are very concerned about this matter. The Nanjing Muslim Cemetery Protection Association sent representatives Jia Guomin and Gai Shaofeng to Shanghai yesterday to report the negotiation process to Hui Muslim compatriots living in Shanghai at the Fuyou Road Mosque in the city at 2:00 pm yesterday (yesterday was the Muslim Jumu'ah day). There were about six or seven hundred listeners.

Haichang Runs Aground; Heshun Breaks Chain and Loses Anchor

Haichang Shipping Company's Haichang, a ship with a deadweight of 955 tons and a draft of 15 feet, is currently sailing to various northern ports. This time, it sailed from Yingkou to Tianjin and ran aground inside the Dagu Estuary due to heavy winds and waves, making it impossible to move. At that time, Datong and Heshun arrived. Haichang asked for help. Heshun had to throw anchor first in the heavy wind and waves, and planned to wait for the wind and waves to calm down before going to rescue. Unexpectedly, Heshun's anchor chain was broken by the wind and waves, and the anchor was also lost, making it impossible to tow Haichang. It had to return to Yingkou. Yesterday, it was confirmed that Haichang had hired another tugboat in Dagu to rescue the ship after the wind subsided.

Aircraft Manufacturing Expert, Mr. Qian Pinsong Returns Home

Mr. Qian Pinsong went to Germany to study at his own expense, and with subsidies from the provincial authorities, in the twenty-first year of the Republic of China. He initially entered Braunschweig University of Technology, and later transferred to Berlin Institute of Technology, majoring in aircraft engines. He also interned for a long time at aircraft engine factories such as Junkers, Hanza, Daimler, and Stettiner, and obtained the title of aeronautical engineer. Two years ago, the Aviation Committee, recognizing his excellent academic achievements, granted him a special subsidy for two years as encouragement. It is reported that Mr. Qian graduated from the former National Peking University of Technology and served as a technician in the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Construction and the Nanchang Municipal Government for many years. After the January 28th Shanghai Incident, Mr. Qian resolutely went abroad to devote himself to the study of aircraft manufacturing, hoping to serve the country. He has now returned home after completing his studies and arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. He went to Nanjing to report to the Aviation Committee and is awaiting assignment. Yesterday, he returned to Shanghai from Nanjing and will soon return to Jiangxi Province to visit his family.

Overseas Chinese Return Home, Scammed in Shanghai: Canadian Chinese Newspaper Records in Detail, Local Authorities Are Requested to Pay Attention

Yesterday, according to a letter from the Huashang Public Bus Company to this newspaper, it received a newspaper clipping from the Canadian New Republic Daily, detailing the scams suffered by overseas Chinese returning home in Shanghai, and attached the original newspaper. The excerpt is published as follows, hoping that those responsible for local security will pay attention.

Comrade Zhang Xinghui, former standing committee member of the Canadian General Branch and editor of the Xinghua Daily, after returning to China from last year, successively served as the director of the Overseas Department of Guangdong National University and a member of the General Branch's Guangdong Office. In recent years, he has devoted himself to education, providing much guidance to overseas Chinese children studying in Guangzhou. Mr. Zhang has been back in China for two years. Due to the restrictions of the Canadian immigration regulations, he could not stay in the country for a long time, so on the sixteenth of last month, he boarded the Japanese Empress ship from Hong Kong to return to Canada, and safely arrived in Vancouver three days ago to disembark. Mr. Zhang is now stationed at the Vancouver General Branch. According to Mr. Zhang, when the ship passed through Shanghai this time, many scammers on the pier pretended to be passengers on the same ship. When they saw overseas Chinese disembarking, they immediately approached them and took them to various places in the city for sightseeing, eating, and buying Beijing glue, Liushen Pills, ginseng shavings, etc. When ordering, they either pretended to forget to bring money or pretended that the money was not enough, put on an act, and then asked you to lend them money to pay, claiming that they would return the money after returning to the ship. At the same time, they handed over the purchased items to you for safekeeping to show their sincerity. After getting the money, they took the opportunity to leave. All those who accompanied them were deceived. Little did they know that the so-called Beijing glue was all cowhide glue, and the so-called Liushen Pills, ginseng shavings, etc., were all fake goods. Only afterwards did they realize their mistake, but it was too late. According to investigations, there were more than a dozen passengers on this trip who were scammed in the same way. Some were scammed out of two or three hundred yuan, and some were scammed out of dozens of yuan. There were big scams and small scams, depending on the amount of money you were carrying to determine their tactics. It is said that passengers on every ship have encountered similar scams in recent years, especially those returning from overseas. Even those who boasted on the ship that they were not easily fooled could not avoid being scammed once they landed in Shanghai. It must be known that the tricks of scammers in Shanghai are novel and numerous. Overseas Chinese passing through Shanghai, if they are not careful, will fall into their trap. Special caution is required. According to investigations, the overseas Chinese compatriots of Canadian nationality, Mr. Situ Tiehun, opened the Lingnan Hotel in Shanghai, Mr. Huang Zhongwen opened the Huashang Public Bus Company, and Mr. Li Mianchen opened a trust company. All of them are honest and reliable. When compatriots arrive in Shanghai, if they ask for guidance on everything, they will be happy to help, so that they can avoid being scammed by scammers.

Lawyer Zhang Zhirang and Others Publish an Advertisement Urging Shi Liang to Surrender, Shi's Mother Faints and Vomits Blood, Her Siblings Also Urge Her to Return Quickly

Ms. Shi Liang was arrested by the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, together with the French Concession police, late at night on the 22nd of last month, because the authorities believed that she had political activities. She was handed over to the Third Branch of the Higher Court and ordered to be released on bail. Initially, the defending lawyers Zhang Zhirang and Tang Hao were responsible for releasing her on bail. Later, after leaving Shanghai for Suzhou, Shi saw a newspaper publishing the Shanghai Municipal Government's announcement of the reasons for the arrest of Shi and Shen Junru and seven others. Shi then fled and failed to appear in court. The Procuratorate of the Third Branch of the Higher Court has issued an arrest warrant and ordered the Procuratorate of the First Special Court to summon lawyers Zhang and Tang to court, ordering each of them to pay 500 yuan in cash as bail and to find and hand over Shi Liang within ten days. This was reported in this newspaper. Now it is reported that lawyers Zhang and Tang and Shi's family have been sending people to search in all directions for days, and [blank] letters to relatives and friends to inquire about her whereabouts, but they have not been able to find any trace of Shi. Shi's mother also fainted, vomited blood, and fell ill after receiving the letter of Shi's escape. Now that lawyers Zhang and Tang have heavy responsibilities and the court deadline is approaching, they published a notice in the newspaper yesterday urging Shi Liang to surrender immediately. Shi's younger siblings Shi Gongzai, Mengyun, and Shuzhi also published a notice in the newspaper yesterday, urging Shi Liang to surrender quickly to comfort their mother, because Shi's escape was causing their old mother great anxiety while she was sick. The two advertisements have already appeared on the front pages of yesterday's Shen Bao and Xinwen Bao and will not be repeated here. It is not known whether Shi Liang, after seeing the newspaper abroad, will surrender immediately.

Dire Market Conditions Make Sustenance Difficult: Tai Feng Company Declares Bankruptcy Again, Court Ruling Approves and Announces

*Shen Shi News* reports: The Tai Feng Canned Foods Company, previously unable to pay its debts due to losses, had once suspended operations. Later, it petitioned the court for a settlement ruling, which was approved, and it resumed business as usual. Now, due to sluggish market conditions, it is difficult to sustain operations and fulfill the terms of the settlement. The company had no choice but to file for bankruptcy, which the court has ruled and approved for declaration. The following is a transcription of Announcement No. 14484 from the First Special District Court of Jiangsu and Shanghai:

Announcement: This court has accepted case No. 29 of the year 25 of the Republic of China, concerning the Tai Feng Canned Foods Co., Ltd.'s petition for bankruptcy declaration. The debtor, previously having suspended operations and being unable to clear debts, petitioned for a settlement, which was approved by this court on November 25th of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Now, according to the debtor, after resuming operations, due to the depressed market and poor business, not only could the settlement terms not be fulfilled, but current operations are also difficult to maintain, and they can only petition for bankruptcy. The court has ruled to approve the bankruptcy declaration. The main text of the ruling, the name and address of the bankruptcy administrator appointed by this court, the address for handling bankruptcy affairs, the deadline for filing claims, the date of the creditors' meeting, and the meeting location are listed separately below. In addition to the known creditors and debtors who will be notified separately, this announcement is made for general knowledge. All creditors must bring supporting documents and file claims at the bankruptcy administrator's office for handling bankruptcy affairs within the filing period specified below. Furthermore, they should attend the creditors' meeting on time for discussions and should not delay. Failure to file a claim within the deadline will result in the inability to receive payment from the bankrupt estate. Moreover, debtors of the bankrupt and holders of assets belonging to the bankrupt estate must not make payments to the bankrupt or deliver their assets, and should immediately return or notify the bankruptcy administrator of such debts or assets. All are required to comply without violation. This announcement is hereby made.

(1) Main text of the bankruptcy ruling and the date of declaration: The ruling was declared on November 23rd of this year. Main text: The debtor, Tai Feng Canned Foods Co., Ltd., is bankrupt as of 10:00 AM on November 23rd of the 25th year of the Republic of China.

(2) Name and address of the bankruptcy administrator, and the address for handling bankruptcy affairs: Accountant Li Ding, residing at No. 133 Yuanmingyuan Road, Room 514; Lawyer Sen Fenling, residing at No. 712, Continental Emporium, Nanjing Road; Lawyer Xu Zuyan, residing on the second floor of the West China Trust Company Building, Jiangxi Road, Beijing Road. The address for handling bankruptcy affairs is located on the second floor of the West China Trust Company Building, Jiangxi Road, Beijing Road.

(3) Deadline for filing claims: From November 23rd of this year to December 31st of this year.

(4) Date of the first creditors' meeting: 2:00 PM on December 23rd of this year.

(5) Location of the creditors' meeting: Hu She, at the intersection of Guizhou Road and Beijing Road.

November 22nd, 25th year of the Republic of China.

Robbery of Wages at Shenxin No. 9 Factory: One Thief Shot and Captured, Box of Legal Tender Unharmed, Investigation and Patrol Prevented Great Loss, Captured Thief Severely Injured and Near Death, Another Thief Escaped Without a Trace

At around 9:00 PM last night, while the Shenxin No. 9 factory on Tokyo Road, Macau Road, in Shanghai's west was distributing wages, two robbers, armed with pistols, who had infiltrated the factory by mingling among the workers, suddenly jumped out and snatched a briefcase containing 1,800 yuan in legal tender from the factory accountant's hand, attempting to escape. However, they were spotted by the factory's investigator and two Chinese police officers employed by the factory. The police opened fire, resulting in one thief being shot in the abdomen and captured, while the other thief escaped during the chaos. The stolen briefcase was completely recovered, and not a single cent was lost. Details follow:

Wage Distribution

The Shenxin No. 9 Cotton Mill at No. 140 Tokyo Road, Macau Road in Shanghai's west, routinely distributes wages to workers on the fourth evening of each month, totaling around two to three thousand yuan. Yesterday was another wage distribution day. Around 9:00 PM, the factory accountant, Mr. Gu, arrived with a briefcase containing 1,800 yuan in legal tender. Another 1,000 yuan was in his pocket, and he went to the factory to distribute the wages by name.

Briefcase Snatching

As Mr. Gu was about to open the briefcase and distribute the money, two robbers armed with pistols suddenly jumped out of the crowd of workers, approached Gu, and threatened him to remain silent. One robber snatched the briefcase from Gu's hand, while the other guarded the rear with a gun. They rushed out of the factory building, hoping to escape through the side gate.

Investigator's Intervention

Previously, several incidents of wage robberies had occurred in the Shenxin factories. To be cautious, the factory had paid special attention to security measures whenever wages were distributed. In addition to the ten Chinese police officers regularly employed to protect the factory, they also increased the number of investigators who guarded the factory day and night in shifts to ensure safety. As the two robbers were escaping the factory building, investigator Liu Chunlan, on the night shift, was patrolling with police officer No. 767.

One Thief Shot

Investigator Liu was shining a flashlight around while the police officer followed with his gun. They suddenly noticed two people fleeing in a panic, and one was carrying a briefcase containing wages. Realizing something was wrong, they shouted for them to stop, but the two abandoned the briefcase and fled for their lives. The police officer fired at them, hitting one of the robbers in the abdomen, who immediately fell to the ground and was captured.

Wages Recovered

The remaining robber took the opportunity to escape through the factory's back door without a trace. Investigator Liu Chunlan and the police officer immediately retrieved the briefcase and returned it to the accountant, Mr. Gu. After checking the contents of the briefcase, they found that not a single cent was missing. They immediately notified the Putuo Road police station, and the police chief dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to rush to the scene. The injured robber was taken by car to the Public Concession hospital for treatment. It is reported that his injuries are severe, and his life is in danger.

Post-Incident Investigation

After the police station's investigation, it was concluded that this robbery was a pre-planned, organized operation. The robbers must have had prior knowledge of the factory to infiltrate it so easily. Furthermore, the escape of the robber through the back door requires further investigation. The back door leads to Moganshan Road. It is usually locked, except when coal is being transported. The fact that the robbers had managed to open the door beforehand to create an escape route indicates that they must have had prior organization and a carefully laid plan.

Female Workers Fight for Freedom of Marriage

Residing at the Women's Relief Association, Father Accuses Her Lover

Teng Kaotang, from Yancheng, resides on Hengfeng Road in Zhabei. His eldest daughter, Jin Gui, is 20 years old and has been betrothed to someone. She and her sister work at the Yutai Silk Factory in Tanziwan. Recently, she fell in love with Yang Zizhen. Because her father disapproved, Jin Gui first hired lawyer Wu Kaisheng to publish a statement declaring her right to choose her own marriage. Fearing that her father would use his authority as a parent to force her, she also moved into the Women's Relief Association, declaring that she would fight for her freedom of marriage, or she would rather not leave. Teng Kaotang became extremely angry and hired a lawyer to sue Yang Zizhen in the district court for abduction, claiming that Yang first seduced his daughter and then, fearing the consequences, incited her to devise this plan as a form of resistance. Yesterday, Judge Shao Qinzhi of the court held a hearing. The defendant, Yang Zizhen, stated that he is from Nanjing, resides at No. 787 Jiaotong Road in Zhabei, and works as a foreman in an iron factory. He denied any adulterous activities. He also said that after the lawsuit, the plaintiff, along with Zhu Zigao and Guo Xiaochu, proposed a settlement, agreeing that neither party would sue. Witnesses Zhu Zigao and Guo Xiaochu testified that the settlement did occur, but the defendant instructed them to settle the matter at lawyer Wu Kaisheng's office. Finally, female lawyer Tu Kunfan, representing Jin Gui, stated that Jin Gui opposed the old marriage system, voluntarily moved into the Women's Relief Association, and hired her to appear in court. She would not return home unless the marriage arranged by her parents was dissolved and she was granted freedom. The judge ordered Jin Gui to appear in court at the next hearing, but she must not be forced to return home. The plaintiff agreed, and the judge ordered the defendant to post a 4,000 yuan bail and await further questioning.

Investigation of Theft Case at Bank of Communications Warehouse Concluded

Sentencing Scheduled

Regarding the theft of 15 large packages of white silk worth over 10,000 yuan from the second floor of the Bank of Communications warehouse at No. 865 Suzhou Road, which occurred on the evening of November 22nd at approximately 9:00 PM, the Hongkou Police Department, led by Chinese detective Feng Qishan, arrested the suspects Kong Qingfu and Liu Jianzhong from Zhenjiang, brokers Xiao Eryi and Xu Wenfu from Shaoxing, and Jin Binhan (detained at the Public Security Bureau) from Shaoxing, residing on Xinmin Road in Zhabei, as well as suspects Jia Shaoyun and Zhu Xiangfu from Zhenjiang, totaling seven individuals. Furthermore, they retrieved the stolen 15 large packages of white silk from the Japanese-owned Sato Yoko at No. 7 Wusong Road and brought them all back to the police station for questioning and detention at the First Special District Court. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police department sent Kong Qingfu, Jin Binhan, and the others to the Third Criminal Court. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu from the Public Concession stated that after investigation, Jia Shaoyun and Zhu Fuxiang were found to be uninvolved and requested their release, which the court granted. Questioning Kong Qingfu and Liu Jianzhong, they confessed that the instigators were Tian Dalian, also known as Da Longbao, and two others who are on the run. They claimed that they were only lookouts. Xiao Eryi confessed that Jin Binhan came to him and said that there were 15 packages of white silk from Wuxi in Shanghai, selling for 800 yuan per package, and asked him to help sell them. He then entrusted Xu Wenfu to sell them to a Japanese, Ke Da, earning a commission of 5 yuan per package, unaware that they were stolen goods. Xu Wenfu's confession was the same, and he claimed that he was introduced to Ke Da by his Japanese friend, Fukuda. Jin Binhan confessed that the white silk came from his friend Liu Changlin and that the fake invoice from his Dacheng Silk Factory was also his. The remaining confessions were evasive. Xiao Eryi and Xu Wenfu hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend them. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that the investigation revealed that the suspects met at the Tongfangju teahouse on Gongguan Road in the French Concession approximately one month before the theft to discuss the plan. Judge Xiao Xieffen ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and scheduled the sentencing for a later date.

All Sectors Promote One-Day Movement

National Goods Factory Association

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association, in order to continue promoting the one-day movement to donate to the anti-Japanese war effort, yesterday sent a letter to all member factories, stating: "The Standing Committee of the Executive and Supervisory Committees held a joint meeting on the 2nd of this month. The Standing Committee proposed a comprehensive plan for resisting aggression and saving the country. With bandits and puppet troops encroaching on our borders and foreign aggression intensifying, and since the recovery of Bailingmiao in Suiyuan province, reports indicate that the puppet troops are actively advancing, attempting to succeed (omitted). The people in our rear are donating funds to support the troops, a trend that is sweeping the nation. The patriotic fervor to resist aggression and save the country has shown a unified expression of the entire nation. How should we decide on a comprehensive plan to support the government, strengthen national defense, and achieve the goal of striving for strength, and how should we first raise funds to support the troops? Please decide." It was resolved that the military affairs in Suiyuan cannot be resolved in the short term. It is now resolved that the employees and workers of the association's member factories should continue to donate one day's income each month until the end of the war against the enemy. The factories are responsible for implementation and external publicity to reach all sectors of Shanghai and proceed uniformly. The record is on file. The case is hereby recorded and you are requested to check, implement it promptly, and report the implementation date for record. Sincerely, to all member factories, implementation methods: (1) Employees and workers should contribute one day's salary each month. The factory should contribute the total salary of all employees and workers for one day to the military expenses until the end of the war in Suiyuan. (2) Donors should send the donations to the National Bank for collection and register the bank receipt with the association for public announcement."

Tenant Association

Yesterday, letters were sent to the Citizens' One-Day Income Contribution to National Cause Promotion Association, the Purchase Aircraft to Celebrate Birthday Association, etc., regarding the fundraising method for the one-day movement in the real estate industry. The original letter stated: "This year is Generalissimo Chiang's 50th birthday, and the fundraising by all sectors to purchase aircraft is extremely enthusiastic. Subsequently, the Chamber of Commerce initiated the one-day movement, and the donation of funds has progressed even further. However, the real estate industry in this city, which owns huge assets, has not yet made any representation. Recently, reports have indicated that all sectors are eagerly hoping that the real estate industry will also rise up and participate in the one-day movement to jointly overcome national difficulties. Our association expresses its utmost sympathy. However, the fundraising method must be appropriate. According to our association's limited understanding, we propose that your association and others be responsible for leadership, designate a bank for payment, and have all tenants in the city pay one day's rent. Tenants can deduct it in the payment of the monthly rent by presenting the bank receipt. The bank should announce it in the newspaper every day to show credibility. If this method is revised and implemented, our association will persuade the tenants to comply. We hereby request that you check and reply."
