(4) Is there any self-treatment?

Answer: (1) Facial capillary congestion. (2) Excitation of the vasomotor nerves. (3) Take "Bromagsin." (4) See (2).

Acid Reflux and Gas

No. 124, Wang Dacheng asks: I often have a very uncomfortable feeling in my abdomen, as if something is pressing down on it. Sometimes I have nausea, regurgitate acid, and regurgitate sour-smelling things. My throat feels numb, spicy, and painful. Two or three hours after eating, my stomach starts to hurt, but it stops hurting if I eat something. Therefore, I would like to ask: (1) What is the illness? (2) Is it dangerous? (3) What should I eat? How should I recuperate? (4) Do I need a stomach wash? (5) What medicine should I take?

Answer: (1) Hyperacidity. (2) No, but it is lingering. (3) Foods to avoid are pepper, chili, scallions, ginger, garlic, alcohol, soda water, vinegar, lemons, hawthorns, coffee, and cigarettes. Foods to eat are eggs, meat broth, milk, potatoes, tofu, and various meats. (4) Wash your stomach with a 1% sodium bicarbonate solution. (5) "Biscama" or "Dioxima."

A Bundle of Miscellaneous Questions

No. 125, Chen Xierong from Fudan Experimental Middle School, Xiangyin Road, Jiangwan, asks: I am sixteen years old and have been suffering from nocturnal emission for eleven years. My body is weak. I have several questions and would be grateful for your answers: (1) Can chest tightness, slight pain, and neurasthenia occur together? (2) There is blood in my sputum, and I am also coughing up blood. I have had an X-ray and percussion, and there are no signs of lung disease. Where is the bleeding coming from? (3) The doctor said, "The bridge of my nose is damaged, and I have nasal congestion, phlegm in the back of my nose, and a lot of mucus." Is this rhinitis or something else? (4) Given the above symptoms, and also suffering from anemia, can I do deep breathing and cold water friction? (5) I dream a lot at night. Is washing my feet with hot water effective? (6) What kind of eye drops are best? (7) What medicine should I take for anemia? What common vegetables are effective? (8) Can I drink cold milk in winter? Is it harmful to eat it after it has been left out for a day? (9) Due to the economic crisis and national crisis, my source of income has been cut off. Can you reduce the fees if I come to you for treatment? (10) How long will it take to cure these illnesses completely?

Answer: (1) These are symptoms of heart disease and can also be accompanied by neurasthenia. (2) Blood from a nosebleed can mix into sputum. (3) The meaning of this sentence is unclear. It is probably chronic nasal mucosal inflammation. (4) These treatments must be appropriate for your body. Forcing yourself to do them may be harmful. (5) Effective. (6) What kind of eye disease do you have? (7) For anemia, take "Livemin." Spinach and carrots contain a lot of iron, which can treat anemia. (8) It is best to eat warm milk to avoid causing gastric catarrh. Milk is nutritious, and eating it after it has been left out for a day is not a problem. (9) Please come and talk to me in person. (10) Nosebleeds and anemia can be cured in a short period of time. Heart disease and nasal disease take time to cure.

Treatment for Blood Deficiency

No. 126, Wang Jin from No. 1155, Yuyuan Road, asks: My body is weak (pale complexion, easily fatigued when working, afraid of the cold in winter...). I consulted a doctor who diagnosed me with blood deficiency. I would like to ask: (1) What kind of blood-tonifying medicine should I take and what kind of blood-tonifying injections should I get? (2) What brand of blood-tonifying injections sold in the market is the most effective and reliable? (3) Do I need to have my blood type tested before getting an injection?

Answer: (1) "Livemin." This medicine is a liver extract preparation. The effectiveness of liver extract for anemia has been recorded in various famous medical journals, and many world-famous doctors have written articles introducing it, so there is no need to elaborate. Liver extract therapy for anemia has now become the standard therapy. Iron preparations from the past have become obsolete. "Livemin" is available in both injectable and oral forms. You can choose one to use. (2) See (1). (3) You need to have your blood tested, but not your blood type (blood type is used for blood transfusions). Instead, you need to have a red blood cell count, a white blood cell count, a blood cell type (are there small blood cells, polymorphic blood cells, giant blood cells, red blood cells with basophilic granules...), and a hemoglobin content test (Cocr Index). The benefit of a blood test is not only that your illness can be accurately diagnosed, but also that it can serve as a standard for treatment. In other words, the clear sign that you do not need to continue treatment is when the red blood cell count returns to 5 million and the hemoglobin content returns to 80%.

Walking into the entrance of "Spring Garden Lane", the first thing that catches your eye is the food stalls lining the street. The vendors are all thin, sallow-faced Chinese, their eyes staring intently at passers-by, shouting at the top of their voices:

—A big one for a dime—

—A big pile for two dimes...

Under the arcades on both sides, philosophers with signs like "Tong Tian Xiao", "Li Banxian", "Guiguzi You Gan Ling" and so on, as if threatened by the economic panic, desperately trying to save their precarious fate, agitate their eloquent tongues and talk loudly about the magic of fortune-telling. Sometimes they are almost like the Shanghai prostitutes, dragging people, and those who don't know are startled by him.

Feeling very thirsty, I drank two bowls of red bean porridge next to a small stall, and then went to watch mahjong. There are five or six "mahjong playing" shops on the short "Spring Garden Lane"! The sound of clapping and banging filled the whole street, giving you the feeling of being in a theater. Each mahjong parlor has at least a dozen tables of players, and some have as many as twenty! The rooms are so small, but they squeeze in patiently. Sixty or seventy people occupy those mahjong tables, leaning their backs or sticking to the walls to satisfy their gambling addiction. The soldiers who come here to participate in the bamboo battles are all unemployed hooligans, coolies, and petty citizens. They put their entire lives on this, and their hopes and fantasies are also placed on this. Looking at how pitifully thin they are, their energy is almost exhausted. Yet they are not awakened, forgetting that they are killing themselves.

Past the "mahjong parlors" are the ice rooms, herbal tea shops, hot and cold food stores, etc., interspersed with each other, occupying almost nine-tenths of the entire street. Everyone knows that Cantonese people are especially particular about "eating" (Cantonese people account for more than 80% of the population here). Every restaurant and food store is "full of seated guests". If you have a few cents in your pocket, you can go to the herbal tea shop for some entertainment, and a dime's worth of tea is enough. You can watch the female waitresses applying rouge and powder, and there are several newspapers to read. If you have more dimes in your pocket, you can spend four dimes to listen to the songs of the famous stage stars. Some people sit with a cup of tea until the store closes.

Walking closer to the dog track, there are teahouses and movie theaters, where you can enter and watch for two hours for a penny.

The Jiaojia Street that runs horizontally through the street is known to everyone as "Weishijie" (Food Street). The name itself suggests that the street displays all kinds of food, and the people who come and go are mostly "for food".

Spring Garden Lane! I spent a lot of time here.

Yan Qi

— Especially

When the early winter drizzle and breeze tightly lock the dry treetops, I think of Yan Qi again.

He had a weathered face, and a short, small beard covered his chipped upper lip. His eyes always liked to squint at people up and down.

He set up a stall at the entrance of our residence, displaying things that easily tempted children's appetites, a colorful pile. You couldn't talk about "hygiene" in that remote street, let alone a small business. Let the mosquitoes and flies of summer suck the marrow of everything, let the wind and sand of winter cover the entire stall, making the goods lose their luster. These were ineffective on the children. After all, those piles and piles would cause the swallowing of greedy saliva!

——Yan Qi, call him, then look at his face, carefully pointing at the glass box: Lend me two cents for cold noodles!

——Lend again? You haven't paid off the last time, do you know? His eyes squinted again, go, go ask your mother for money to buy it!

A thought quickly floated in Xiaoxinyan's mind, "Asking for money" is not an easy thing. Fine! You dare not lend me, you'll get yours. At this point, he ran back and called a few partners from the same courtyard. Little Maotou and Little Wu were also invited. When they came out, the momentum was a little different. They surged up and asked him if he would lend them or not. He didn't put these little ghosts in his eyes at first, so naturally he wouldn't "yield". In this way, we all united and turned our mouths up, imitating his appearance, drawing our fingers across our faces——

——Look, the glutton who stole meat was cut with a knife, chipped, pfft! pfft!

He didn't want this shortcoming to be on the children's lips. Keeping a beard also had a considerable connection to this. Using this weakness, we attacked him. In order to avoid extra publicity, in the end, we were able to easily satisfy our own desires.

Time is fast, two years are like a gust of wind, gently passing by.

It's spring, everything is overflowing with "the vitality of life", but Yan Qi is deeply locked in sorrow. Depression stimulated his nerves, and he often mixed up the accounts of loans. We knew that there must be endless hidden pain in his heart, but he refused to say it, but the degree of worry gradually deepened.

After that, a child appeared next to his stall, about five or six years old, calling him Dad. How? Didn't he have no family? In the past two years, whether directly or indirectly, we had never heard that he had a child.

From that time on, problems arose with his stall. Sometimes it was set up as usual, and sometimes it could be closed for several days.

It was a late autumn night, and the Meifu Line kerosene lamp on the stall was burning, its light radiating in all directions from the glass cover, strangely dim, accompanied by the desolate street, even more showing a sense of desolation. A woman in her thirties sat next to the stall, her complexion quite ugly, and there was an unapproachable, bleak atmosphere between them.

Then, he didn't set up his stall for more than ten days. This creditor of the children often aroused inexplicable concern. The harsh wind of early winter swept across the residual leaves on the earth, and the fine rain mixed the muddy streets into a muddy porridge. After the lights were lit, it was said that someone was stabbed in Nanhuawozi. It was said that the injured person was Yan Qi, who set up a small stall. The injury was very serious, and his life was in danger.

Why? I don't know. Some say it was a love killing, some say it was revenge, and some attribute it to fate!

From then on, his stall was no longer seen on the street. Ah, we still owed him some odd bits of account! The dry treetops were tightly locked by the early winter wind and rain again. Therefore, I thought of Yan Qi again, but eight years had already passed.

Movie

Star Magazine

"Vigorous" Full of Northern Atmosphere "Eternal Smile" Working Hard

Xu Xinfu's new work "Vigorous" still appears in the form of a passionate detective film, the script comes from Hong Shen's hand, writing about a solemn story in the black smoke of the Northland, starring Gu's Lan Junmei Jun sisters and Wang Zhengxin, You Guangzhao, Wang Jiting, Shu Xiuwen, Yao Ping, etc. With Xu Xinfu's proficiency in producing such films, the tidal force of the whole play is enough to boil the audience can be expected. All the sets, props, costumes and even the characters' forms in this film are full of strong northern atmosphere. After the brutal emotion of "Vigorous", smart viewers will definitely see who the gang it is targeting!

"Eternal Smile" is directed by Wu Cun, written by Liu Na'ou, and is a more elaborate work by Hu Die following "Women's Rights", writing a tragic story about a singer on the Qinhuai River. Gong Jianong, Gong Qiuxia, Wang Xianzai, Shu Xiuwen and others co-star. Mr. Wu Cun's handling skills are vivid, beautiful and full of emotion, creating a more beautiful and fresher style of Chinese film, and Hu Die is confident to build her own style in this film, she understands the singer Yu Yuhua in this "Eternal Smile" thoroughly, she will very carefully build this saint-like female type. "Eternal Smile" is currently working hard.

Noma Xila Plays Juliet in "Casting Love"

Guanle Food Company Expanded Opening Specially Invited Chen Juanjuan to Cut the Ribbon

Guanle Food Company, located at Xiafei Road, Hualong Road, has been established for five years and is famous in the French Concession for its food and Cantonese cuisine business. Recently, with the daily prosperity of the business, the company's board of directors has been planning to expand, enlarging the storefront, adding more than ten rooms to the Cantonese restaurant upstairs, and hiring artist Zhang Yunqiao to design, decorating for three months, and the project was completed the day before yesterday, and it coincided with the fifth anniversary, so the expansion opening ceremony was held on the morning of the 5th of this month, and the little star Chen Juanjuan was invited to cut the ribbon, and refreshments were prepared to entertain the guests, and at the same time, a large price reduction and large giveaways were held to give preferential treatment to all sectors of society as a memorial, and it is expected that there will be a lively scene at that time.
